I beg you to observe." The Southwest Executive Committee of the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang kowtows. (September 2nd, East India)

Ministry of Finance Newly Establishes Provisional Regulations on Export Tariffs 80

Beijing News - The Ministry of Finance promulgated the following provisional regulations on export tariffs by ministerial order: (Article 1) For goods subject to ad valorem export and transit duties, the average wholesale market price at the time of customs inspection in the local area shall be used as the dutiable value. This average wholesale market price shall include the cost of packaging and sorting the goods, but taxes shall not be included. If there is no average wholesale market price available for examination at the port of export, the average wholesale market price of other major domestic markets may be used as the basis for calculating the dutiable value. (Article 2) For goods exported to foreign countries that have already been sold under contract, the genuine contract listing the selling price of the goods shall be presented together with the customs declaration. The contract may be regarded as proof of the price of the goods, but it is not necessarily regarded as conclusive proof. The interpretation of this point shall be at the discretion of the customs. In addition to requiring merchants to present contracts, the customs may also use all effective methods at will, such as checking other documents related to assessment and valuation, investigating detailed sales documents, examining merchants' books, inspecting goods, and, when necessary, engaging in all interviews and inviting any private individuals to assist in determining the dutiable value. (Article 3) If the exporter is dissatisfied with the price, classification, tax amount, or fees set by the customs, he may submit a written protest to the Customs Commissioner within 20 days after the customs declaration or other customs registration is filed, clearly stating the reasons for the objection. Before the case is resolved, the merchant may submit a deposit and request that the goods be released first. The amount of the deposit shall be sufficient to pay the fixed amount of tax and other additional taxes set by the customs, but this method is limited to those approved by the customs. Within 15 days after receiving the protest, the Customs Commissioner shall re-examine the case. If it is believed that the merchant's protest is unreasonable, the case shall be submitted to the Inspector General of Customs for review. If the Inspector General of Customs finds that the Customs Commissioner has handled the case appropriately, it shall be forwarded to the Customs Administration for review and determination by the Tariff Classification and Valuation Review Committee. (Article 4) When the Tariff Classification and Valuation Review Committee meets, all issues concerning procedures, etc., shall be decided by a majority vote. The majority vote shall be submitted to the Customs Administration for approval and promulgated within 15 days (excluding holidays) for unified compliance. (Article 5) If the Tariff Classification and Valuation Review Committee determines that the actual price of the goods in dispute over the price exceeds the number originally declared by the protester by 20% or more, the customs may, in addition to collecting the normal tax payable, order the protester to pay a fine of 10 times or less the amount of tax concealed. (Article 6) If goods that have been sold under contract and are subject to price disputes have not been presented with the contract when declaring customs, the contract will not be recognized as proof of the price of the goods if it is presented to the Tariff Classification and Valuation Review Committee in the future. The protest will be deemed invalid.

Li Yunjie's Division Recovers Nanfeng - A Detailed Account 81

Zhu Penglin's Factions Routed at Guangchang

Peng Dehuai's Elite Troops Eliminated

Nanchang Dispatch: Zhu Penglin (Biao) and Ji (Zhentong)'s four factions recently invaded from southern Jiangxi. Except for the Pseudo Fourth Army Corps guarding their base, the Pseudo First, Third, and Fifth Army Corps were concentrated in Yihuang. Luo Binghui's Pseudo Twelfth Army seized Nanfeng from Guangchang and plundered Nancheng, aiming to jointly attack Fuzhou. Fortunately, Chen Cheng and Wu Qiwai's armies, passing through Chongren and Lean from western Jiangxi, emerged southwest of Yihuang and recovered Yihuang. Seeing their route to Ningdu from Lean cut off, the bandits retreated south in two directions: one retreating via Huangpi near southeastern Yicheng towards Qia Village in Nanfeng, and the other detouring west of Nancheng to enter Nanfeng. From the 2nd, Chen Cheng, the front-line commander, led his divisions to advance towards the bandits in Nanfeng and Guangchang from Nancheng and Yihuang, while strong forces remained in the rear of Yihuang to search for remaining bandits and maintain order. Military sources report that Li Yunjie's division on the left wing first stormed into Nanfeng city on the 3rd, killing over a thousand bandits. Luo Binghui's Pseudo Twelfth Army, defending the city, retreated towards Ganzhu and Kuzhu in Guangchang. Li's division's staff office sent a telegram to the province yesterday, reporting the recovery of Nanfeng, which reads: "Our division arrived at Lita on the evening of the winter (2nd). At dawn of the next day, we, along with Xu's division, launched a general attack on Nanfeng County according to the original plan. The defenders of Nanfeng were Luo Binghui's troops, numbering 40,000, who relied on fortifications and resisted stubbornly. Fortunately, our officers and soldiers were brave and fierce, and with a determination to die, charged repeatedly without losing heart. The bandits were greatly demoralized and feared that Xu's division would outflank them, so they fled towards Guangchang in disarray. Before leaving, they looted and burned the city, causing over a million yuan in losses to the people, a truly unspeakable suffering. In this battle, over a thousand bandits were killed, and a large amount of military supplies were captured. Special notice is given." The Political Training Department of the 24th Division also telegraphed a report on the recovery of Nanfeng, stating: "Mao Bingwen, Li Yunjie, Xu Kexiang's divisions besieged Nanfeng at dawn on the next day. The bandits resisted relying on fortifications. After fierce fighting for several hours, they occupied Nanfeng city at 3 PM. Many bandits were killed, and countless military supplies were seized. The bandits are retreating towards Guangchang, and our army is in pursuit." The Political Training Department of the 5th Division also telegraphed a report, stating: "The Pseudo Third Army Corps' 2nd and 3rd divisions were besieged by our 14th Division in the northwestern mountains of Yihuang on the winter and next days. On the next day, the bandits attempted to flee west, but Wu Qiwai's army was searching from west to east, resulting in a pincer attack. Over 500 bandits were captured, along with over 400 rifles and 5 light and heavy machine guns. The 5th Division arrived at Tangyin and discovered that Peng's troops were still hiding in Dongkeng Mountain, 15 li from Tangyin. The bandits near Tangyin fled southwest on the next day upon hearing the news. In the morning, the 5th Division searched and eliminated the remaining bandits in the vicinity, capturing over ten bandits and seizing 4 rifles. Our armies are continuing the search and pursuit." From this, it is evident that the remaining bandit troops will not be able to hold out for long.

Another report: The Jiangxi bandits' attempts to flee to Fujian and Guangdong were unsuccessful, and they retreated to the southern Jiangxi area, where their situation is extremely dire. At this time, the Commander-in-Chief of the Jiangxi-Guangdong-Fujian Border Area剿匪總司令ordered all units to strictly blockade the bandit areas, causing the bandits to perish without being attacked. Knowing that it would be difficult to survive, the bandits recently gathered the remaining forces and launched a full-scale invasion of Lean, Yihuang, Nanfeng, and other places, hoping to join forces with Fang Shao's bandit troops in eastern Jiangxi and disrupt Fujian and Zhejiang. Fortunately, the National Army met them head-on with a severe blow. Recently, the elite 1st and 2nd divisions of Peng Dehuai's Pseudo Third Army Corps were completely eliminated in the Yihuang area by the National Army's 28th and 4th Armies, which intercepted them separately. Lean, Yihuang, and Nanfeng were successively recovered. The bandits suffered extremely heavy losses and are now fleeing back to their lairs in disarray.

Dissolution of the Communist Bandits in Southern Jiangsu and Northern Anhui 82

Communist Bandits Launch a Major Riot in Xiao and Ling Counties

Local Militia and Police Join Forces to Pursue and Attack

Bandit Leaders Wang Xiaobai and Others Captured

Xuzhou Dispatch: In the northern Anhui counties of Su and Ling, popular uprisings occurred last month due to the collection of opium seedling taxes. When the Su County uprising first started, Communist leader Wang Xiaobai participated. At that time, farmers were being oppressed by corrupt gentry and local bullies. Wang Xiaobai called for the liberation of the farmers, which gained him the support of many rural villagers. He was elected as the commander-in-chief. Afterwards, the Su uprising was quickly resolved. The opium tax was exempted, saving farmers a total of over 2.3 million yuan in opium taxes, and the local area also gained considerable benefits. Seeing that the farmers were living peacefully and could not be exploited, Wang Xiaobai purely engaged in Communist activities. On the one hand, he took advantage of the conflict between the old and new factions in Su County. When the Su authorities were surrounded by the old faction and planned to arrest the leaders of the rioters, Wang instigated farmers to riot. On the other hand, he gathered party members and formed bandits to cause disturbances, operating between Su, Ling, Xiao, and Tong counties. At that time, all four counties sent police squads to prevent and block them. As for the farmers who were incited by Wang, they elected Wang as the commander-in-chief, and Communists Zi Yimin, Xu Huaizhen, and others were appointed to important positions. They gathered about 200 direct descendants of the Communist Party and united with Wu Xueming, the leader of the Wuji Dao, leading 400-500 members of the Red Spear Society to concentrate in northern Ling County. On the 1st of this month, they attacked Shicun. Shicun was a large town, and after a fierce battle all day, it was not captured. Shicun is an important area where Xiao and Ling counties meet, and it is close to Xiao County. Upon receiving the report, Xiao County Magistrate Wang Gongyu personally led a police squad to Chulan Town on the 2nd and proceeded to Zhangshan Town along with the 10th District Defense Corps of Xiao County to block and suppress the bandits. The bandits then abandoned the attack on Shicun on the 3rd and traveled overnight to Langanshan stronghold, intending to detour through Shixiang and deploy forces in the Phoenix Mountain area to cut off the Xiao County police squad's return route. Later, County Magistrate Wang learned of this plan and immediately led his team back to Chulan on the 4th. When bandit Wang realized that his plan had been exposed, he led his cadres around to Meishan near Chulan, while Wu Xueming led the Red Spear Society to Yutaishi and Linkou to hide. Just in time, the Tongshan County police squad arrived and blocked them at Taoshan and Yangzhuang. At the same time, the 9th Division also sent a team to Yusi to suppress them. County Magistrate Wang then led the entire police and defense corps to attack bandit Wang's cadres at Meishan. However, that area belonged to Ling County, and the villagers, incited by bandit Wang, expressed dissatisfaction with the Xiao police suppressing bandits across the border. County Magistrate Wang then stopped advancing further. Bandit Wang also fled to Daqingtong Mountain on the border of Xiao and Ling counties on the evening of the 4th, gathering his followers in Xiangqiao, Mafu, and other villages. County Magistrate Wang again led his team to track and pursue them. From dawn on the 5th to the afternoon, the bandits' strength was unsustainable, and they completely collapsed. The police squad then captured three Red bandit leaders, Wang Xiaobai, Xu Huaizhen, and Dou Yimin, and captured about 50 bandits, seizing more than 40 rifles and pistols and killing dozens of bandits. The gang was then sent to Chulan Town. The minor offenders were dealt with on the spot. Wang, Xu, and Dou were escorted to Xuzhou by County Magistrate Wang on the evening of the 6th and sent to the garrison headquarters for interrogation. County Magistrate Wang returned to Chulan on the 7th to handle the aftermath. Currently, the Communist bandits in southern Jiangsu and northern Anhui have been resolved. It is reported that Wang Xiaobai is a native of Su County, about 30 years old, and once studied at Peixin Middle School, which was run by the Xuzhou Christian Church. (7th)

Record of a Journey West (17) 83

Brief Situation of Luochuan

Luochuan covers an area of about 170 li east to west and about 200 li north to south, with a population of about 40,000. The county has more than 7,000 mu of cultivated land and more than 2,000 mu of barren land. The annual tax revenue is about 23,000 yuan from land tax, 18,000 yuan from surcharges, and 3,500 yuan from miscellaneous taxes. On the expenditure side, education expenses are about 7,300 yuan, the Public Security Bureau 4,800 yuan, the Finance Bureau 1,030 yuan, the Construction Bureau 1,030 yuan, the judiciary 1,800 yuan, and miscellaneous items 2,800 yuan. There are two senior primary schools, with about 220 students, one senior girls' primary school with about 37 students, and 95 junior primary schools with a total of about 1,400 students. In addition, there is also a public primary school. Tuition is not charged for any of these schools, but the senior primary schools receive about 2,000 yuan in public subsidies each year, the senior girls' primary school 1,000 yuan, and the public primary school 100 yuan. The expenses of the junior primary schools are fully borne by the local communities separately. Teachers' salaries are about 10 to 22 yuan per month for senior teachers and about 5 to 8 yuan for junior teachers. Cotton is grown on about 300 to 400 mu of land, with each mu yielding 30 jin. The cotton seeds are all domestic because American cotton seeds are not suitable for the local soil. The quality of the cotton is very good, and the fibers are also long. The county uses more than 80,000 jin of cotton each year, and the amount of cotton produced is not enough for local use. A veritable black cloth belt.

Shaanxi has three coal-producing areas: Guanzhong, Hanzhong, and Yulin. According to investigations by the Shaanxi Construction Department, the reserves are estimated at over 3,153 trillion tons in the Guanzhong area, 490 trillion tons in the Hanzhong area, and 1,116 trillion tons in the Yulin area, totaling 4,729 trillion tons. The northern figures are reduced and compromised numbers, and many omissions remain. The types range from peat, lignite, bituminous coal, semi-coal, coal gas, candle coal, and anthracite to graphite. Nothing is missing. The candle coal of Mian County is particularly unique. It resembles the Dakiji coal of Shanxi and the super white coal of England in appearance, and it burns very quickly with a long, strong flame, making it ideal for steamships and warships. In addition, the mines are very shallow, the engineering is simple, and projects can be started with funds of any size and produce results immediately.

Songjiang 84

Provincial Party Headquarters Sends Personnel to Inspect Social Education Institutions

Zhang Mingshun, dispatched by the Provincial Party Headquarters, arrived in Songjiang today, tasked with investigating whether social education institutions are making efforts to promote Party doctrines and how their work is progressing. Fengxian 85

Efforts Begin to Clear Old Land Tax Arrears: The old land tax arrears in this county are quite substantial. Although the Land Tax Arrears Committee has cleared them several times, it has been unsuccessful due to poor management. Currently, local communities believe that if this continues, it will not only affect national tax revenue but also cultivate bad habits among those responsible for tax collection. Therefore, they have specifically submitted this matter to the current local administrative meeting, re-electing Chen Xiaochu, Lin Bocui, Shao Keren, and four others to form a clearance committee and reorganize it. It was formally established yesterday. In addition to the mutual election of Ruan Xiyao as executive secretary, responsible for organizing the work, accountant Fan XiongGuang has also been hired as the chief auditor. The clearance methods stipulate: (1) The chairman of the committee shall be the Director of the Finance Bureau, and, when necessary, representatives from various agencies may attend and participate. (2) The clearance sequence shall be divided into two phases, with the period from 1927 to 1931 as the first phase and the period before 1926 as the second phase. (3) All files and account books related to the land tax shall be sent by the Finance Bureau at any time, and a list of the serial numbers and collection tickets for each year shall be reported for review. (4) The amount of old arrears cleared by the committee each year shall be announced in the newspaper. If it is confirmed that a clerk or official has embezzled funds, the committee shall request the county government to order a limited-time recovery. (5) The clearance period shall be limited to two months, and the expenses shall be temporarily disbursed from the current year's contingency fund by the estate management office in the amount of 500 yuan, which shall be deducted and returned from the old arrears found in the future.

Jiangyin 87

Logistics Officer of the Anti-Smuggling Team Commits Suicide: The 9th Brigade of the Anti-Smuggling Team stationed in Cheng, now renamed the 5th District Team, is stationed at Zhang Yuantai Salt Warehouse in Puhui Bridge. The team leader, Xie Chunting, was suffering from carbuncles and was being treated at the Fuyin Hospital. The team affairs were mainly managed by logistics officer Shen Guicang (Qiuyan). Xie Chunting went to Shanghai to attend a meeting of the Salt Affairs Tax Police Bureau, secretly attempting to seek a position as a district chief, but was unsuccessful. After returning to Cheng, he was greatly agitated. At 3 a.m. on the 6th, he suddenly stabbed himself in the left and right temples with a bayonet, causing his brains to burst out. He also stabbed himself in the chest. He was rushed to the Fuyin Hospital for treatment but died. At 4 p.m., the team collected the body and telegraphed Minhang to notify his family to come to Cheng to collect the coffin and return to their hometown.

The Deputy Village Head Was Kidnapped but Rescued and Escaped Danger: Zhu Zhengshan, deputy village head of Qiren Village, Shazhou in the 3rd District, has been a traditional Chinese medicine practitioner for many years. At around 9 p.m. on the 5th, five or six bandits went to Zhu's house under the pretense of seeking medical treatment, mistakenly going to Zhu Peisheng's house next door. They left a letter demanding 1,000 yuan. When Zhengshan heard the noise, he knew something was wrong and quickly escaped through the back door. He was spotted and caught by the bandits, who dragged him towards the North Gate. Fortunately, the 3rd Independent Platoon of Deji Street heard about it, and the platoon leader, Liu Xinpei, led his men to chase after them, recovering the hostage. The bandits fled towards Siwei Port.

Military Police Search and Suppress Ambush Bandits: A local gang of bandits in the eastern countryside of Nantong has colluded with pirates and become very rampant. Gunfire can be heard everywhere at night. The military police and the magistrates of Tong and Hai counties have jointly decided to search and suppress the ambush bandits. On the 7th, County Magistrate Zhang rushed to various districts in Yudong to command the operation.

Investigate and Prohibit the Collection of Boat Fees: When Jiangnan steamships arrive at various ports in Tong County, the shipping bureau sends boats to disembark passengers, and the Public Security Bureau sends police to collect boat fees from passengers on the ships, charging 20 cents per passenger. The 4th District Headquarters of the Water Police believes that this matter is a disturbance to merchants and travelers and is prone to danger, so it has sent a letter to the county government to investigate and prohibit it.

Encouraging Wealthy People to Donate Funds: Tong County needs to provide 80,000 yuan for the food and requisition of mules and horses for the 25th Route Army. The county government has requested and obtained approval from the provincial government to encourage wealthy people to donate funds to offset the expenses.

How should this be effectively implemented? Zhenjiang 90

Zhenjiang Establishes a Property Transfer and Tax Collection Office: In this province, the transfer of property rights and the transfer of tax obligations among the people in various counties are handled by the Zhuangshu, Ceshushu, and Zhoushu offices in each county. However, there are many drawbacks. At the Provincial Government's 519th meeting, Finance Department Director Shu proposed that each county establish a property transfer and tax collection office. This was subsequently approved by the 520th meeting, and the regulations were promulgated, requiring each county to establish the office by September 1. It is now learned that the Zhenjiang County Finance Bureau, upon receiving the order, immediately sent personnel to prepare for the establishment of the office. The office was established on September 1, and all land tax registers have been transferred back to the Finance Bureau for management. Fearing that the villagers in various villages and towns are not yet aware, the regulations and the Zhenjiang County Government's joint announcement of the establishment of the property transfer and tax collection office will be posted. In the future, all private transfers of property rights in this county must use official contracts and personally go to the Finance Bureau to pay the transfer tax, transfer the tax obligation, and issue official seal certificates as proof of business. If anyone still collects taxes privately through bookkeepers, it will be invalid once discovered.

Daosheng Money Shop Robbed by Bandits: At around 7 p.m. last night, seven or eight thugs suddenly arrived at the Daosheng Money Shop next to the Qianye Guild Hall on Xiwu Street in this port. They wore different types of clothing and were armed with weapons. Two of them stood guard at the door, while the rest swarmed inside, drew their pistols, threatened to silence them, and forced the shop staff to hand over the location of the hidden silver. The shop staff were forced to hand over the key to the silver cabinet, which contained 2,379 yuan in banknotes, 40 yuan in silver dollars, and 80 cents in small silver coins, all of which were robbed. An employee named Wang Mingruo was injured on the cheek by a pistol butt. During the search, there were three silver ingots inside, which were old and black. The bandits thought they were lead and ignored them. Before leaving, they locked the shop staff in a room and left. A moment after the bandits left, the shop staff dared to go out and report to the Public Security Bureau and the headquarters of the Detective Team and the Business Corps. However, the bandits had already disappeared without a trace.

Bandits Rob and Rape: At around 3 a.m. last night (5th), three bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Wang Cunde, a resident of Baishui Alley on Nandajie in this city. Autumn Tide Sinks River Boats: The western Xing bank of Xiaoshan has recently been hit by a large autumn tide. On the morning of the 7th, the tide was several zhang high. Two river boats were unable to avoid the tide and were destroyed. Two firewood boats traveling upstream in the Qiantang River were sunk by the tide near the Six Pagoda Temple, drowning two male and female boatmen. Attempts were made to rescue them at the time, but due to the large waves and rapid current, it was impossible to rescue them. It was not until the afternoon that a male body was recovered in Wenyan. The female body has not yet been found.

The Elimination of Traitors Corps Uses Bombs to Warn Traitorous Merchants: The anti-Japanese associations have discovered several tens of thousands of yuan worth of enemy goods in the post office. After identification, it has been confirmed that they are indeed enemy goods. The public corps held a meeting on the 3rd and decided to completely burn them. The location and date have not yet been determined. However, Tongfeng Store in Sipaolou North originally mailed 80 pieces of enemy goods. The anti-Japanese associations only discovered 15 pieces. It is reported that the remaining 65 pieces have been smuggled to other ports. The Blood Soul Elimination of Traitors Corps sent repeated letters to the store, limiting them to transport the goods to the Party headquarters for identification by the 3rd, but they were ignored. The corps was furious and hung a bomb on the store's door on the 3rd. The store did not dare to open for half a day. It was not until the afternoon that an officer removed the bomb, and the store resumed business as usual.

Special Education News

Future Reforms Needed in Education 94

(2) Zhang Angqian

3. Emphasis should be placed on production education. Our country has always had the saying "scholars are noble" and "those who labor with their minds govern others, those who labor with their bodies are governed by others." Because these old ideas are not easily broken, and because education has not been able to exert its social role, it often turns out that those who are educated are those who do not produce. This is especially true for educated women, who often see education as nothing more than a tool for gaining vanity. Therefore, graduates of various schools today tend to flock to the teaching profession, forming a circular education phenomenon. As a result, the longer the period of education, the higher their desire for life increases, and the more isolated they become from the production undertakings of society and the country. Is this not contrary to the Three People's Principles of education, which clearly aims to enrich the people's lives, support the survival of society, develop the national livelihood, and continue the life of the nation as the greatest goal? Therefore, from now on, we must pay attention to increasing vocational subjects in schools at all levels, attach importance to labor practice, introduce the ideas of public production and shared enjoyment, and cultivate the spirit of teamwork. We must integrate education with society, hoping to achieve the realm of "education is life" and "education is production." Only then can we say that we are increasing domestic production and reducing domestic consumption. Only then will the power of education to save the country become more truly apparent. 4. Military education should be vigorously implemented. I still remember that in the early years of the Republic of China, our primary and secondary schools all had a gun drill subject. Recently, it has changed to emphasize only unarmed exercises. Although since last autumn, there have been new facilities for military training in middle schools, specialized schools, and universities, it is feared that these are only formalities due to the urgency of the matter. When the Shanghai War broke out, hundreds of people actually volunteered to sacrifice themselves for the country on the front lines. Unfortunately, the total number of people was too small to be of much help. I hope that from now on, all primary schools will focus on health exercises, especially Boy Scout training. In addition to intensifying Boy Scout training in secondary and higher schools, military training should also be vigorously implemented. Those who fail the military training should not be allowed to graduate. If this is done for several years, I dare to believe that today's students will all be loyal and brave patriots in the future. Once there is a disturbance on the border, they will definitely step forward and organize student armies to be the vanguard of the people, preventing the enemy from crossing the Lei Pool boundary by even one step. Only then will the power of education to save the country become more sufficient.

Alas, deep worries inspire sages, and many difficulties revive a nation. Looking at the Franco-Prussian War and the Russo-Japanese War, it is enough to prove that education is not only enough to save the country, but also to revive it. Therefore, what should educational colleagues who bear the mission of tomorrow's China do?

Let us pledge to work together diligently to fulfill our responsibilities, so as not to fail the expectations of our country and nation! (The End)

Zhu Jiahua Meets with Chiang to Discuss Education Plan in Bandit Areas 95

Announcement of the Dean of the College of Science and Education of National Central University 96

Screening Exam to be Held Starting from the 10th

Nanjing, 8th - National Central University announced on the 8th that Sun Hongfen was appointed as the Dean of the College of Science. Before Sun arrives at the university, Professor Li Ziqing will be temporarily responsible for the affairs of the college. Huang Jianzhong was appointed as the Dean of the College of Education, and Gui Zhibo was appointed as the Director of the Library. National Central University announced on the 8th that the student dormitory has been repaired and will be open to all at 2:00 PM on the 12th, and the rules for入住 were stipulated. Second-year students will live in the first dormitory, third-year students in the fifth dormitory, fourth-year students in the third and second dormitories, and physical education students will live in the east half of the third dormitory. National Central University decided to hold a screening exam starting from the 10th. The screening exam schedule has been announced. The screening exam will be held in groups and is expected to take about ten days.

The resolutions of the Screening Committee of National Central University were announced on the 8th: (1) All students who formally studied in the second semester of the 20th year must participate in the screening. Those who do not participate without reason will be considered as withdrawn from school. (2) The examination subjects are limited to the courses taught in the second semester of the 20th year. (3) All fourth-year students of the 20th year must pass the screening before they can be issued a graduation certificate. Those who are far away or sick and cannot return to school to participate in the screening will be allowed to issue a study certificate temporarily, but they must still return to school next year to participate in the graduation exam. (4) Those who cannot participate in the screening exam due to illness must present a doctor's certificate for verification, but they must take a supplementary screening exam when they return to school. (5) Students who were on leave of absence in the first semester of the 20th year and request to return to school will be exempted from the screening exam. (6) First-year students who were on leave of absence in the 20th year must return to school in the next year. (7) Students who were on leave of absence in the second semester of the 20th year and request to return to school will be exempted from the screening exam, but those who have a lack of 成績 in the first semester due to special circumstances must take a supplementary exam after returning to school. (8) Borrowed students, except for students from Northeastern University and students who have returned from studying in Japan, should transfer back to their original schools and do not need to participate in the screening exam, but if they need 成績, they must take the same screening exam as the students of this school. (8) Auditing students, special auditing students, and probationary students do not need to participate in the screening exam. (10) The exam period will start from the 10th.

The Municipal Education Bureau Cracks Down on Schools Falsely Claiming to be Registered 98

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau recently found that some private schools that have not been approved for registration have the bureau's registration mark on their school plaques or enrollment advertisements, intending to falsely claim to deceive the public. It is reported that the bureau has formulated measures to crack down on this and will first publish a notice in the newspaper, requesting immediate corrections. If they continue to violate the rules, they will be closed.

The Affiliated Elementary School of Qinghua Middle School, founded by lawyer Feng Shuhua, has been established for more than six years. It has never solicited donations from outside, the school spirit is orderly, there have never been any strikes, and the curriculum is serious and the discipline is strict. Even an hour of homework is not allowed to be missed. Therefore, the Education Bureau has specially approved its registration. In addition to continuing to maintain the original serious spirit and good school spirit this semester, more attention will be paid to formal equipment and major renovations. The faculty and staff have also been reassigned. It is reported that Ma Zhangnan, a Bachelor of Arts from university, has been appointed as the Director of General Affairs, Qin Hegao, a Party Ideology teacher from the 3rd Shanghai Municipal Session, has been appointed as the Director of Training, Chen Shenghe, a Bachelor of Arts from Guanghua University, has been appointed as the Director of Academic Affairs, Qiao Pingren, a Bachelor of Science in Mathematics and Physics from Datong University, has been appointed as the Director of the Department of Mathematics and Physics, Zhu Douying, a historian, has been appointed as the Director of the Department of Chinese Studies, and Bao Zhenya, a graduate of St. John's University, has been appointed as the Dormitory Supervisor. In addition, Jin Dicen, a Bachelor of Commerce from Guanghua University, Xu Minhui, a Bachelor of Education from Hua Nan Women's College, Guo Tiaomei, a graduate of the Finance and Commerce Vocational School and a former teacher at Soochow No. 2 Middle School, and Yan Yiyi, a graduate of the Department of Engineering from Jiaotong University, have been newly hired as teachers. Lu Zhichang, Zhu Guang, Wang Songnan, Yang Yongshang, and others have been appointed as registered accountants and school doctors. Classes have already started. It is reported that there are still a few vacancies in junior high school, senior elementary school, and junior elementary school grades three and four. Night school is scheduled to start on the 10th.

China Wins the Robert Cup International Doubles Tennis Final 101

Yesterday, Portugal was Eliminated in Straight Sets

The final is scheduled to be against England this Sunday

The Robert Cup International Tennis Doubles Tournament was held yesterday at the China Tennis Court for the semi-finals between China and Portugal. Although tickets were sold for 6角 per person, the audience still reached six or seven hundred people. Chinese players Qiu Feihai and Lin Baohua defeated Portugal's Kanavalo and H. Kolasa with scores of 6-1, 8-6, and 6-4. China has thus won the final. The final is scheduled to be against the British team at the French Club this Sunday. The situation of the Robert Cup and the progress of yesterday's competition are as follows:

United States Portugal 3-0 Portugal China 3-0 China Germany England 3-0 England Final on Sunday

Qiu and Lin Started Very Smoothly: China's Lin Baohua served first, and the ball was as heavy as a cannonball, achieving miraculous results every time. In addition, Qiu Feihai's net interception focused on Kolasa's offense. Although the Kolasa and Kanavalo were steady and resilient, they ultimately achieved nothing. After China won four consecutive games, Portugal finally won one game. As a result, the Chinese team won the set 6-1, which was extremely easy.

Portuguese Players Focused on One Side: The two Chinese players, Qiu and Lin, are both good at the right court, but not good at the left court. The Portuguese players noticed the weakness and focused their attack on the left court, and their momentum was very fierce. Therefore, the set suddenly became tense. Portugal even used high balls to attack the rear of Lin and Qiu, but the gains and losses were balanced. Portugal took the lead with a score of 2-1. After Lin and Qiu added two games, the situation changed. But Portugal also added two games, making it 4-3, with Lin and Qiu behind. Then it became 5-4, 5-5, and 6-5. The Portuguese players took the lead step by step, with a momentum to complete the game in one go. Lin and Qiu resisted cautiously, and their net interception was very skillful. The Portuguese players used their old trick again, hoping to use high balls to hit the rear of Lin and Qiu, but many balls went out of bounds, resulting in a score of 6-6. After Lin and Qiu captured this pass, their spirits were lifted. They won two consecutive games and ended the set with a score of 8-6.

Wonderful Performances Completed the Gong: The competition in the third set was the most exciting. Kanavalo served, which was very lonely. Lin and Qiu smashed four shots, all of which went out of bounds. The Portuguese then got the first game. Qiu lost another game due to his weak serve. Fortunately, he immediately won back two games. Kanavalo served, and Lin and Qiu lost four balls in a row again. The Portuguese players won the game with a score of 3-2. After reaching 3-3, Lin and Qiu took the lead. In the eighth game, the competition was particularly fierce, with ties for seven or eight times, either short-range or long-range challenges. The Portuguese players sometimes returned the ball with a high ball, and Lin and Qiu respected them with a high pressure. The situation was tense, with mutual gains and losses. Kanavalo focused on intercepting the net on the left court, achieving many victories. However, Lin's serve was also a major problem for the opponent, and Qiu's net placement was often ingenious. As a result of the game, it still belonged to Lin and Qiu. After each added a game, the score became 6-4, and Lin and Qiu completed their mission.

The China-England Final on Sunday: After China eliminated Portugal, it won the right to the final against England. Although the pairing of Lin and Qiu is like adding flowers to brocade and a perfect match, the British players De Fu and Huiter are both famous doubles players, which is very strong. The final between the two teams will be held at the French Club this Sunday, and Lin and Qiu are not allowed to visit.

German Advocates for Football in the Next Alimbeek Games 104

Because European Football Matches are Very Common

They Must Help Economically at the Games

Reuters London, 7th - The next World Alimbeek Games will be held in Berlin, Germany in 1936. The German Organizing Committee is strongly advocating for the restoration of football as a competition item in the next Games. At the same time, the competent authorities of various European countries have inquired about matters concerning the participating teams. The reason for restoring football matches is because football matches are felt to be a very common sports competition in Europe, and they must help with the economic problems of the Alimbeek Games. According to this edition, there are no football matches in Los Angeles.

The Big Problem is Subsidizing Players

| Opinion of the President of the French Football Association |

Remede, President of the French Football Association, published an opinion in the "Otto" newspaper, saying that although the International Alimbeek Committee is against subsidizing football players' time loss, if the United States agrees to have this competition, the committee will definitely abandon its opposition. Football is not very common in the United States, so it will not affect the economy of the Games. In 1928, the International Football Association requested subsidies for football players' time loss, but the International Alimbeek Committee did not agree with this principle, and the organizing committee of the Games claimed that if there were no football matches, the success of the Games would be damaged. The attitude of the Alimbeek Committee has changed, so it is believed that if the organizing committee continues to insist on the principle of subsidizing players' time loss, it will definitely be accepted at the time.

China Youth Initiates Women's Volleyball League 107

Registration Starts Today, Deadline is the 15th

Competition Starts on the 17th of This Month

Now that the autumn is cool and the air is refreshing, volleyball is the most suitable sport. The Chinese YMCA has previously held a men's volleyball league with satisfactory results. The association has always paid close attention to women's sports. Because women's sports in our country are still in their infancy, it is not enough to achieve results without actively promoting them. Therefore, taking advantage of the opening of various schools, the women's volleyball league has been initiated. Registration starts today and ends on the 15th of this month. Each team is limited to 14 people, and must pay a registration fee of 2 yuan at the same time. The competition will start on the 17th of this month. After that, it will be held every Saturday afternoon in the association's gym. This year's single round-robin system will be adopted. When necessary, the scores will be divided into Group A and Group B. The championship team of this year will be awarded a silver cup by the association.

Local News

Minister Song Returned to Shanghai from Haizhou Yesterday 109

The Ministry of Finance Rectifies the Salt Administration of Northern Jiangsu

400,000 Yuan for Dredging Rivers

1,000,000 Yuan for Building Salt Barns

According to the Central News Agency, Minister of Finance and Acting Premier Song Ziwen, considering that the Haizhou area of ​​Northern Jiangsu is the largest salt-producing region in our country, is determined to rectify it and plans to establish salt barns (i.e., salt warehouses) in the area to centralize production, prevent smuggling, and increase tax revenue. Therefore, he specially took a Sikorsky aircraft the day before yesterday, accompanied by Zhu Tingqi, Director of the Salt Affairs Department and concurrently Chief of the General Auditing Office, and Huang Chun Tao, Secretary of the Ministry of Finance, to inspect the Haizhou area and review the Tax Police Corps under the Ministry of Finance. He returned to Shanghai by the original aircraft at 3:30 p.m. yesterday and gave the following conversation to the Central News Agency reporter:

Inspection Situation: Mr. Song and his party departed from Shanghai by plane on the morning of the day before yesterday and arrived in Haizhou at 12:00 noon. They inspected the salt districts of Xinpu and Dapu in Haizhou. They stayed in Haizhou City that night and went to various salt districts for inspection again at 7:00 a.m. yesterday. At 12:30 noon, he accompanied Director Zhu, Secretary Huang, and Commander Zhao of the Tax Police Corps back to Shanghai by the original aircraft. At 3:30 p.m., they arrived safely at Hongqiao Airport, where they were greeted by Mr. Song's guards and took two cars to return to his private residence on Qiqi Road.

Mr. Song's Speech: After Mr. Song got off the plane, the Central News Agency reporter immediately asked about the situation of the salt district inspection and the rectification policy in the Haizhou area of ​​Northern Jiangsu. According to Mr. Song, he believed that the Northern Jiangsu area was the most important salt-producing region in our country, so he specially accompanied Director Zhu and others to fly to Haizhou and other places to inspect the new salt fields and review the Tax Police Corps stationed there. Mr. Song was tired from the journey and needed to rest urgently, so he asked the reporter to go along for details. After arriving at Mr. Song's residence, a secretary who accompanied Mr. Song on the inspection told the reporter about the Ministry of Finance's salt affairs rectification situation.

Rectification Plan: According to the talk, the area inspected this time was Xinpu, Xinpu, and Dapu in Haizhou. Other areas could not be inspected one by one due to time constraints. Haizhou is located on the coast of the Yellow Sea, Xinpu in the east, and Dapu further east. Xinpu and Dapu are both rising grounds, and many new salt fields have been built. Northern Jiangsu is the richest salt-producing area in our country, and the salt produced in the Haizhou area is even more excellent. Dapu is the terminal of the Longhai Railway, so the salt production can be sold smoothly in several provinces. However, in recent years, due to the rise of bandits in the area and the obstruction of transportation, sales have been hindered, and tax revenue has also decreased. The Ministry of Finance has planned a fund of 1.4 million yuan for the rectification of salt affairs in Northern Jiangsu, with 400,000 yuan for dredging rivers to facilitate transportation, and the remaining 1 million yuan for the construction of salt barns. Salt barns are warehouses for storing salt, which will centralize all production to prevent smuggling and increase tax revenue. The salt barns that have been built in the area include five large salt barns and four small salt barns. After the completion of the project, the salt tax can be greatly increased.

Reviewing the Tax Police: The Tax Police Corps under the Ministry of Finance, led by Commander Mo Xiong, went to Haizhou and then went to various places to suppress bandits. According to local people, the bandit situation near Haizhou was so severe that there was a risk of being robbed by bandits 50 steps outside the city of Haizhou. Since entering the bandit suppression, the bandit forces have been reduced, and the residents are safe. However, the regiment suffered some casualties due to its efforts to suppress bandits. One battalion commander and one company commander have died in battle. As for Commander Zhao, who accompanied Mr. Song to Shanghai, he took leave to return to his hometown in Shanghai. Mr. Song has not yet determined the exact date of his return to Nanjing.

Silent Mourning at Noon

Memorial Service Held

The September 18th Incident in the Northeast Province, in the blink of an eye, is the anniversary. After Ariyoshi's Visit to China, Direct Sino-Japanese Negotiations are Widely Rumored 111

But Diplomatic Figures Observe

Saying it is Japanese Diplomatic Tactics

According to the Guowen News Agency, regarding the issue of direct Sino-Japanese negotiations, since the arrival of the new Japanese Minister to China, Ariyoshi Akira, the rumors have been rampant. The Japanese Minister has stated that direct negotiations between China and Japan are possible, but the Chinese government and the public have expressed that it is still too early. The reporter yesterday specially visited an important figure in the diplomatic circle and asked whether direct negotiations could become a reality. According to the answer, the ill feeling between China and Japan has a long history. Before the January 28th Incident, there was a trend of direct negotiations. Later, due to the arrogance of the Japanese side, China appealed to the League of Nations, believing that justice belonged to us, and waited for a solution. Now that the League of Nations General Assembly is approaching, Japan has sent Ariyoshi to China to carry out direct negotiations in order to ease the international atmosphere. This is just a diplomatic tactic of Japan towards China. In short, it is not appropriate to talk about direct negotiations before the League of Nations General Assembly is held. The reporter then inquired about the latest news of the case from foreigners. It is heard that Ariyoshi is in contact, and if there are no major changes in the middle, direct Sino-Japanese negotiations can be realized before and after the League of Nations General Assembly. Let's record it for confirmation.

Jin Wensi has arrived in Shanghai from Peiping 112

Scheduled to go to Europe on the 20th

According to the Far East News Agency, Jin Wensi, the former Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, has not taken office as the Minister to the Netherlands after being appointed by the National Government because of his weak body and unfamiliarity with overseas life. However, after the September 18th Incident, Jin Wensi felt that the country was in extreme danger and should not sit idly by. When the League of Nations Investigation Team came to China, he risked his life and accompanied Dr. Gu Shaochuan to go out of the customs with the League of Nations Investigation Team, experiencing all kinds of hardships. This time, the League of Nations Investigation Team handled the result report in Peiping. The Chinese side's reports and memorandum reached more than 50 pieces, all of which were reviewed and drafted by Mr. Jin together with Mr. Gu. Now that Mr. Gu is going to France as an envoy and will represent the National Government to participate in the League of Nations meeting to be held in Geneva, and strive for the Northeast issue, Mr. Gu asked Mr. Jin to go to Geneva at that time to assist him. Mr. Jin has arrived here by train from Peiping the night before yesterday and is scheduled to go abroad by the British ship Rauchi on the 20th, first to Marseille and then by train to Geneva. His wife will travel to Europe with him and is preparing for the trip. The reporter of the Far East News Agency specially drove to visit Mr. Jin's residence yesterday. Here, the important points of his conversation are recorded below: (Reporter: Mr. Minister, you came here from Peiping. Can you tell us about the current situation in North China? (Mr. Jin replied) Although the current situation in North China is in a dangerous situation, it is not as prevalent as the rumors outside. It is like the sea a few days ago, which is also in a state of alarm, but so far there has been no change, which shows that the rumors are not reliable. The Japanese army has learned a profound lesson from the previous Shanghai war and feels very bored. Therefore, in addition to carrying out various demonstrations everywhere to achieve its ambitions for political action, it has no great significance. However, North China is still maintained by Mr. Zhang Xueliang, and all generals are absolutely obedient and obey his command. (Question) Japan's invasion of Rehe is becoming more and more urgent. Is there a saying that it will launch a large-scale attack on September 18th? Did you hear about it in Peiping? (Answer) Japan has been planning for Rehe for a long time. The pseudo-organization's map has long included Rehe Province. A large-scale attack is only a matter of time, so it may not be on September 18th. (Question) Then what are the authorities of Rehe and Hebei planning to do about this? (Answer) Of course, they are preparing to resist, but the specific measures are military secrets, and outsiders cannot know. (Question) What arrangements is Japan making for the upcoming League of Nations meeting? (Answer) This is really difficult to know, but it is expected that it will ignore everything and be tough to the end. (Question) What is the purpose of Ariyoshi's visit to China? Is it true that he will conduct direct negotiations with the National Government? (Answer) Ariyoshi is the Japanese Minister to China. Before the Sino-Japanese diplomatic relations are severed, it is a very common thing for the two countries to send ministers to each other, and it cannot be said that he is conducting direct negotiations. However, Ariyoshi recently made a statement, in which he said, "I hope that the Chinese side will observe and resolve the Sino-Japanese dispute with a long-term vision," etc. This is really no different from saying that our government can quickly recognize the Manchurian pseudo-organization as a buffer zone for the Sino-Japanese struggle, so as to eliminate ill feeling invisibly and gradually increase the friendship between the two countries. The so-called long-term vision can be explained by this. This kind of remark is absurd. His main mission here can be imagined by this. (Question) What is your opinion on direct negotiations? (Answer) Direct negotiations are not equal to betraying national sovereignty and humiliating the country. For example, when two people are in dispute, they must first reason with each other. If they do not follow the right path, they will fight each other. When fighting still cannot be resolved, then they will ask a third party to intervene. The so-called reasoning and the so-called mutual fighting are all direct negotiations. Therefore, the so-called directness is a necessary step. However, our country has lost the opportunity for direct negotiations at present. After the Shenyang Incident, the Japanese were afraid of intervention by various countries, so they eagerly sought direct negotiations to end the matter. However, the public was deeply afraid that the government would betray the country and strongly opposed it. By now, the Japanese forces in the Northeast have been deeply entrenched, and the pseudo-organization has been established, and there is no room for further direct negotiations with me. Therefore, observing the current attitude of the Japanese, they actually want our country to negotiate with the pseudo-organization, which is what our people can tolerate. Finally, Mr. Jin told the reporter again that the focus of diplomacy has shifted to the League of Nations, and the focus of the League of Nations is actually in the United States. Therefore, in the future, I hope that the comrades in the press can pay attention to this point, and strive to advocate friendship in the Sino-US relations. Moreover, we should establish a strong and independent proposition to express our own definite attitude. If we ourselves cannot have a strong expression, even if a third party wants to help, there is no way.

Japanese Residents Still Trying to Oppose the Implementation of the Consular Visa System 119

Since our Customs announced the implementation of the regulations on consular visa for cargo transportation on September 1st, foreign merchants in Shanghai have shown no opposition, but Japanese merchants are still actively opposing it, and have falsely cited five points as reasons for their opposition. Details of each item are recorded below:

Requesting Japanese Minister to Negotiate: The Japanese Chamber of Commerce, various road business associations, the Textile Federation, and other commercial organizations have held meetings for days to discuss countermeasures against the consular visa system announced and implemented by our government. Since the new Japanese Minister to China, Arima, arrived in Shanghai, their activities have become even more active. On the day after Arima's arrival, Yasui, the acting administrative chairman of the Japanese Residents' Group, Ichimachi, the vice president of various road business associations (because the president, Hayashi Yoshiwo, has not returned from Japan), and others, representing all Japanese merchants in Shanghai, met with Arima and requested him to propose the abolition of the consular visa system to us. The outcome is unknown due to the confidential nature of the content.

Reasons for Japanese Merchants' Opposition: As a result of the Japanese merchants' meetings for days, the following five points have been decided as reasons for opposition: (1) The procedure is troublesome and hinders trade with China. (2) The system is a means of resisting Japanese goods. (3) The visa fee is excessive and places an excessive burden on Japanese merchants. (4) The system is, in fact, a disguised increase in tariffs. (5) Chinese consuls stationed abroad are corrupt and untrustworthy. If the consular visa system is allowed to be implemented, Japanese merchants will be subjected to a major oppression in the future. In addition to the above five items, there are also various other absurd remarks to confuse foreign merchants and hope to achieve their conspiracy.

Failure to Contact Foreign Merchants: Before the Shanghai Customs announced the implementation of the consular visa system for overseas consuls, Japanese merchants in Shanghai had already expressed obvious opposition, and even published a letter to friendly foreign merchants, hoping to contact merchants from friendly countries to take unified action against it. However, foreign merchants generally believed that our new system had sufficient reasons, and that tariffs had already been autonomously set, so there was no room for opposition. Therefore, they all rejected the Japanese rhetoric and followed the new system. It is said that Japanese merchants have realized that this plan has completely failed and have decided to take individual action in an attempt to make a final struggle.

Protesting the Establishment of Branch Offices: Since the Ministry of Foreign Affairs announced the establishment of consular branch offices or offices on September 1 to expedite the consular visa system, our Ministry has successively sent personnel to Osaka, Kobe, Taiwan, and other places in Japan to prepare for the establishment of branch offices. They have now all been declared established and have begun issuing cargo transportation certificates. However, the Japanese government has used the excuse that our Ministry of Foreign Affairs did not obtain Japanese consent in advance to establish branch offices in the aforementioned places and intends to order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to protest to us, demanding its cancellation. It is also said that this proposal is also a suggestion contributed by Japanese merchants in Shanghai to the Japanese government.

Representatives from Various Places Arrive in Shanghai: For the purpose of collectively deliberating on appropriate measures to oppose our implementation of the consular visa system, Japanese commercial organizations in Tianjin, Qingdao, and Ping are said to have sent representatives to Shanghai to negotiate everything. After the representatives from various places arrive, Japanese commercial organizations in Shanghai will hold a "Joint Conference of Japanese Merchant Representatives from Various Places" on a scheduled basis to discuss the method in detail.

Another Twist Arises

According to the Dagong News Agency, after the entire staff of Xu Chongdao announced a general strike, they decided to resume work at 8:30 am yesterday after repeated persuasion by representatives of the Party Department. Resumption of Work: All employees went to each branch of the head office at 8 am yesterday and worked as usual. Unexpectedly, the management posted a notice in the head office stating that it was necessary to dismiss Cen Yongkang, Zhou Gang, Zhong Jiren, Yang Xikui, Shao Bingxiang, Sun Zhengkui, and six other leaders of the strike, which caused dissatisfaction among all employees. The group representatives Zhong Jiren, Yang Xikui, and others went to the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union to request negotiation. After the union convened an emergency meeting of directors and supervisors, it was decided to petition the Party and government agencies.

Petitioning the Party and Government: Zhao Zhenhui, Fang Qingjian, and other members of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union, as well as Yang Xikui, Zhong Jiren, and other representatives of the Xu Chongdao group, went to the Party and government agencies at 11 am yesterday to petition, stating that the management violated the principle of resumption of work and dismissed six workers without reason, requesting strict prohibition. Section Chief Xu Yefu of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau received them and promised to be responsible for negotiating with the store and not to violate the principle of resumption of work or cause other disputes. Later, the representatives went to the Municipal Party Department to petition, where Director Wang Manyun of the People's Training Section received them. After inquiring about the situation in detail, he immediately sent staff member Li Weibing to the store to negotiate.

General Assembly: After the employees followed the instructions of the Party Department yesterday morning and went to work in various branches of the head office, the store unexpectedly posted a notice wanting to dismiss Cen Yongkang and six other employees. They immediately sent representatives to report to the union, requesting strict negotiations, and decided to hold a general assembly at the Second District Branch at 9 pm last night to discuss countermeasures.

Union's Statement: According to the person in charge of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union, who told the Dagong News Agency reporter, the entire staff of Xu Chongdao reluctantly accepted the persuasion of the Party and government and resumed work as ordered. Unexpectedly, the management believed that the strike was illegal and insisted on dismissing the six instigators, which caused dissatisfaction among all employees. It was found that before the resumption of work, four principles had been decided with the management, but they were now violating them without reason, going back on their word, and the responsibility should be borne by the management. In short, the union sincerely hopes to settle the matter and does not want to cause further incidents. If the management does not understand the difficulties and insists on dismissing them, the union will not hesitate to sacrifice everything and lead all the pharmaceutical workers in Shanghai to support the employees of Xu Chongdao.

Store's Attitude: The entire staff of Xu Chongdao Chinese Medicine Store automatically and unconditionally returned to work at the store at 8:30 am yesterday. The labor unrest was resolved as reported. However, the store is still strictly investigating the leaders who instigated the strike. Once the facts are verified, it will still be reported to the Party and government authorities for legal punishment.

News on Labor Disputes at the China Merchants Electric Company 125

Due to labor disputes at the China Merchants Electric Company, former executive members Zhu Hanhe, Tang Junsheng, Zhou Guangrong, Zhang Ruoyu, and other workers had temporarily requested leave and stopped working. The company and higher authorities have mediated between the two sides for many days, but a real solution has not yet been reached. It is now learned that the inspectors on leave, Zhu Hanhe, Zhou Guangrong, Zhang Ruoyu, and the driver Tang Junsheng, returned to the company yesterday to cancel their leave and work as usual. Unexpectedly, at around 4 pm, someone suddenly threw dirty objects at inspector Zhu Hanhe at the corner of the Shanghai military camp, and then an incident occurred, and the tram stopped for a short time. Also, it was reported that the China Merchants Electric Company Trade Union had expelled Zhu Hanhe, Zhou Guangrong, and four other事務工 from the union for disrupting the union's actions and requested the company to dismiss Zhu Hanhe and the four others. The company stated that the Party and government authorities had long forbidden the evil precedent of dismissing workers because they were expelled from the union, so they could not open this precedent and replied to the union in a letter. Yesterday, Zhu Hanhe and others canceled their leave and went to work at the company, and a group of workers returned their copper badges to the company, expressing their unwillingness to cooperate with Zhu and others. Rumors spread, and the situation was quite serious. Union representatives Fu Chongde, Tan Honglin, and others relayed the workers' intentions to the company. It is heard that the China Merchants Electric Company still believes that the standard for dismissing employees should be whether they have committed serious misconduct in their service to the company. Otherwise, employees will lose their security and everyone will be in danger, which is not good for the workers. If labor disputes damage the company's business, the company will only take legal self-defense actions. It is said that the workers have not yet agreed.

The Suiyang Steamer Caught Fire 127

The Ship's Hull Was Not Damaged, and the Passengers Were Safe

The Swire Group's Nan Wah liner Suiyang was on its way from Shanghai to Qingdao on the afternoon of the 7th of this month. When loading kerosene at the Guanghua Wharf, a fire broke out in the third cabin due to carelessness, destroying a batch of goods. The ship returned to Shanghai, and the situation is reported as follows:

The Suiyang Steamer, bound for Qingdao, came to Shanghai from Hong Kong and Guangdong and entered the port on the 4th of this month. After unloading the goods, it was berthed at the Huatong Wharf in Pudong. On the 7th, it loaded export goods in Pudong and set off for Qingdao. This time, the goods transported by the ship to Jiaozhou were mainly paper and tea. The loading was completed at 2 pm on the 7th, and it set off for the Guanghua Kerosene Wharf in Gaolousha to transport kerosene to Qingdao.

Fire Broke Out in the Third Cabin: At about 4 pm, the Suiyang Steamer arrived at the Guanghua Wharf. After berthing, it opened the cabin to load oil. Unexpectedly, when the third cabin was opened, flames emerged from the cabin, indicating that a fire had broken out due to carelessness. Once the cabin door was opened and the air circulated, the fire suddenly erupted on the deck. Captain Barron immediately ordered all sailors and wharf workers to assist in using the ship's own firefighting equipment to try to put out the fire. However, the cabin was mostly filled with paper, and the fire was fierce and difficult to extinguish.

Customs Rescue: Because the fire was so fierce and difficult to extinguish, the captain hoisted a flag to warn. The Customs received the report and quickly sent a fire boat and firefighters to assist in the rescue. The Fire Brigade also sent fire trucks to assist in spraying water. At about 5 pm, the fire in the third cabin was extinguished. The cause of the fire is still unknown. It is probably caused by a worker leaving a cigarette butt and embers when loading the goods. Swire Group also sent personnel to the ship to inspect.

Returned to Shanghai: After the fire in the ship was extinguished, the burned goods and the water-damaged goods had to be unloaded to the wharf, and the notary had to evaluate the number, etc. Therefore, the Suiyang Steamer could not sail to Qingdao again. Swire Group ordered it to return to Shanghai and still berth at the Huatong Wharf in Pudong. It was found that there were more than 2,700 pieces of cargo in the third cabin, mostly paper, but there was also tea. Yesterday, the burned paper was unloaded onto the wharf, and the loss of tea in the water-damaged goods was still small and could still be shipped by the original ship.

A Glimpse of the Losses: The loss of the burned goods was quite large. Swire has now notified the guests to first handle the摊水, and the amount of damage still needs to be investigated and estimated before it can be known. The hull of the ship was not damaged, but it needs to be repaired, so the export was postponed to the 10th. When the fire broke out, the passengers on the ship were able to safely disembark because the ship was berthed at the wharf and it was in the afternoon. After the embers were extinguished, they boarded the ship again, so there was no panic.

The God of Wealth Temple Lawsuit 128

Donor Sues Incense Keeper's Wife for Encroaching on Property

Court Orders Clarification Before Further Hearing

On Wuding Road in western Shanghai, there is a public Temple of the God of Wealth, which has a long history. During the late Qing Dynasty, in the thirty-first year of the Guangxu era, the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau filed a lawsuit against a Mr. Zhu who lived in the temple, claiming the temple was public property. However, they did not win the case, so Mr. Zhu remained in the temple. For more than twenty years since then, no further disputes arose. After Mr. Zhu died, his wife, Ms. Tan, continued to manage the temple. Recently, Ms. Tan renovated the temple and applied to the Land Bureau for a land license, which aroused opposition from Wu Zongjun, Xi Hongde, Zhang Facan, Tan Deming, Wu Xingeng, Xu Xingen, and others who claimed to be donors to the temple. They all stated that the temple was a local public temple, and that Ms. Zhu Tan actually wanted to drive out the Taoist priests in the position of an incense keeper, which no one could tolerate. Therefore, they hired lawyer Hong Shihao to file a lawsuit against Ms. Zhu Tan. The complaint stated: "The public Temple of the God of Wealth at 32 Wuding Road, originally named Yingxi Convent, was built by public donation from local believers and has a considerable history. Records from various ancient books since the Qing Dynasty show this clearly. The miscellaneous affairs within the temple have been managed by incense keepers hired by the temple owners. From the time the plaintiffs' ancestors donated funds to establish the temple until now, they have worshipped at the temple from time to time. They have only required the incense keepers to not neglect their duties and have not closely supervised them. Over the years, this has become a habit. However, they have never given up their shared right to the temple property. Unexpectedly, the defendant, who has long received the plaintiffs' kindness and relied on them for food and shelter in the temple, dared to covet the temple property in the position of an incense keeper. The defendant took over from her predecessor as the incense keeper and managed the temple affairs. Unexpectedly, over time, she became lax and turned from guest to host, regarding the public property as her own. She repeatedly attempted to deceive the land administration office to obtain a land deed. Seeing that the words 'public' were inscribed on the top of the land temple, making it impossible to justify her claim to private ownership, she did not hesitate to fabricate the absurd name of Zhu Gongli to fulfill her ambition to seize public property. She even brought lawsuits to court against fellow incense keepers. The defendant has now brazenly claimed that the public Temple of the God of Wealth is her own and is currently engaged in construction. Given this deliberate plan, the plaintiffs, for the sake of the public interest, cannot remain silent. Therefore, they have filed this lawsuit, earnestly requesting a judgment confirming that the property is a public temple property and granting a preliminary injunction to prohibit the construction of houses or other dispositions before the conclusion of the case, in order to avoid complications with third parties and difficulties in execution in the future." Yesterday afternoon, Judge Shen Hong of the First Special District Local Court held a hearing. The defendant was defended by lawyer Zheng Wenkai. Lawyer Zheng argued that the plaintiffs' accusations lacked concrete evidence, and that the plaintiff representatives, listed in the complaint as one hundred and seventy people, had not provided detailed addresses or occupations. He then debated with the plaintiffs' lawyer, Hong Shihao, and presented evidence. Judge Shen then questioned the plaintiff, Wu Zongjun, and, because the other plaintiffs' statements were the same as Wu's, did not summon them one by one. He ordered a postponement for a thorough investigation and set a date for a continued hearing.

Shortening the Shanghai-Lanzhou Air Route 129

Xi'an-Lanzhou Section Temporarily Suspended

The trial flight of the Eurasia Air Line has been temporarily suspended due to unfavorable weather conditions. However, the original Shanghai-Lanzhou line is part of the entire Eurasia line and has already been in operation. According to the Eurasia Aviation Company authorities, the No. 6 aircraft, flying from Lanzhou to Beijing last week, crashed due to prolonged rain, water accumulation at the airport, loose ground, and unfavorable weather conditions. The aircraft was damaged, and the passengers suffered minor injuries. The company has now decided to temporarily suspend the Xi'an-Lanzhou section. Once the aircraft is repaired and the weather improves, the flights will resume according to schedule. The Shanghai-Nanjing-Luoyang-Xi'an section will continue to operate as usual according to the schedule, without any changes. The rumor that the decision has been made to suspend passenger services on this line is not true. Except for the Xi'an-Lanzhou section, which is suspended, the rest of the line is still operating as usual.

Cutting Off Water Supply Disregards Residents' Lives and Security

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association yesterday responded to a request from the 10th District Branch of the Citizens Federation of Shanghai by sending a letter to the Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession, stating: "We are writing to you regarding a letter from the 10th District Branch of the Citizens Federation of Shanghai, which states that members of the association, Chen Jingshen and He Le, and others from Changkang Lane, Zhoujiazui Road, received a notice from the Water Company on the 26th of last month stating that their landlord, Zhang Shaotang of Fengyi Company, had not paid the water bill and that the water supply would be cut off. The members did not pay attention to this because the landlord is responsible for the water bill. Unexpectedly, on September 2, the water supply was suddenly cut off. When they immediately questioned the landlord, they learned that he was using the non-payment of the water bill as leverage in the unresolved rent reduction issue. The members, because water is essential for life, immediately raised three hundred yuan for the July water bill and sent it to the Water Company, requesting immediate water supply. Unexpectedly, the company refused to accept it, disregarding the lives of the residents. Therefore, we are writing to you regarding this matter. The Water Company's obligation is to provide water to the residents, and its right is to receive water bills. Now that the water bill has been sent and not accepted, and the water supply has not been continued, the suspension of the water supply is only an excuse for the non-payment of the water bill. In fact, it may be under the direction of the landlord. This not only violates the contract between your Bureau and the Water Company, but also creates problems for human morality and public order. Based on the above, we respectfully request that your Bureau promptly order the Water Company to collect the water bill and quickly restore the water supply to maintain the lives and health of the residents."

It is close to the Shanghai Railway Station, and the disaster situation during the recent catastrophe was extremely severe. The tenants requested that the landlord provide the same treatment as other lanes in the vicinity and waive rent for four months. The landlord only agreed to three months, which led to a dispute. The two sides insisted on their positions. The landlord filed a complaint with the Local Court, ordering them to pay off the arrears and vacate the premises. The tenants took the old rent for January to the court for payment, but the landlord refused to accept it, demanding that four months of old and new rent be paid at once and that everyone must vacate the premises. On September 3, the court was requested to seal up Wang Xiangtai's woodworking shop, and it was said that if the arrears were not paid off immediately and the premises vacated, everyone would be sealed up, causing great public anger among the tenants, who wanted to take drastic action and fight the landlord. The association did its best to dissuade them and mediated the dispute, but the landlord refused to agree.
