In terms of human feeling and justice, it is truly heartless. The tenants' request for a four-month rent waiver is not an exceptional demand. The other lanes in the vicinity, such as Huide Lane, Huachang Lane, Shende Lane, and the Tianbao Lane and Nanlin Lane south of the railway, all automatically waived rent for four months. The Beizhu Fan Lane even waived four and a half months. The Zishou Lane next door waived four months and then reduced rent by 30%. Is the disaster in this lane less severe that they must waive only one month less? Moreover, the landlord is not a puppet and should consider when the Japanese troops withdrew from Zone B. It is against humanity and justice to be so unreasonable. Wang Xiangtai's arrears are only for one month, which does not count as arrears before January 28. These tenants cannot be said to be bad. The arrears of the new rent were caused by the rent waiver dispute and are the landlord's own doing. Furthermore, the Municipal Party Headquarters is still petitioning the Central Government to revise the rent waiver standards, and various rent reduction associations have notified the tenants to postpone rent payment before the standards are officially established. According to these regulations, Wang Xiangtai's arrears do not exceed the limits, but his shop was sealed up, which is unreasonable. Stepping back, it is feared that Wang Xiangtai may be unable to pay the arrears and may flee secretly, so a preliminary attachment was made. However, there is a guarantor to pursue. In summary, the landlord is completely unreasonable. At a time when rumors are rampant and people are uneasy, the businesses in the disaster areas are half-dead and stagnant, and the common people are struggling to make a living. How can they withstand such great oppression? If the government does not impose appropriate sanctions immediately, others will follow suit and evict tenants or ask the court to seal up their shops to satisfy their desire to increase rent. If this continues, the association can say with certainty that there is no hope of recovery, and the Zhabei market will decline and never recover. A strong enemy is invading from the outside, and the landlords are destroying from the inside, forcing the common people to have nowhere to live. Thinking of this, how can we not be filled with emotion? Therefore, we earnestly request that the landlord be severely punished and that the court be ordered to unseal Wang Xiangtai's shop to appease public anger. The rent arrears should be paid according to the old rent, and the new rent should be paid in installments. We also request that all landlords be ordered that, unless the Zhabei houses are actually taken back for their own use, they are only allowed to recover rent arrears and are not allowed to evict tenants at will. In this way, people's hearts will be at peace, and there will be hope for recovery. The above is a direct statement, respectfully requesting your consideration. Lu Youguang, Chairman of the Zhabei Shilu Businessmen's Association."

Kunlun Winery Increases Production 136

Foreign wines flood the market, mostly from Europe and America. Imports reach 30 to 40 million yuan annually. The outflow is not small. Overseas Chinese Li Xiang and others, in view of this, in the eleventh year of the Republic of China, gathered overseas Chinese merchants to prepare to set up a factory. In the summer of the twelfth year of the Republic of China, the factory was established with a registered capital of 150,000 yuan. Because it used the spring water of Huishan Mountain to brew wine, it set up a factory in Wuxi. In the autumn of the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, it set up a general distribution office in Shanghai and branches in Guangzhou. However, the initial products were not easy to sell and were squeezed out by imported goods. The business losses were quite large. It then continued to raise new shares of 150,000 yuan from overseas Chinese and moved the factory to Tangshan Road in Shanghai. All matters of the company were reformed, and Dr. Mei Guantao, a chemistry doctor, and European and American winemaking masters were hired to assist in everything. In recent years, the products have become more and more excellent, enough to compete with imported goods, and the price is especially cheap, several times different from the price of imported goods. Recently, with the increasing sales, the supply is in short supply, so the production has been increased. In addition to the original four types of brandy, such as Samsung, Five Star, Blue Seal, and Longevity, three types of port wine, such as Hero, Samsung, and Kai Di, and red wine and white wine, new products have been added, such as Gold Medal and Silver Medal whiskey, which are all praised by people in society. The company's winemaking machine strength can produce about 300 gallons of wine per day. The raw materials used to be 60% to 70% from foreign countries, but now only 20% to 30% are used. The technical progress is truly a rare achievement in domestic products.

International Trade Bureau Calls Meeting of Ham and Egg Industry Yesterday 137

Discussing Concrete Measures to Deal with Philippine Government's Tax Increase

The International Trade Bureau, because ham, eggs, sausages, lard, and other items in the city are bulk foods sold abroad, and the Philippine government recently increased the tax rate on ham, eggs, and other foods, convened a meeting of relevant exporters at the City Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 p.m. yesterday to discuss countermeasures. Representatives of the City Chamber of Commerce, Luo Qinghua, Cai Xiaohe, representing the Ham Industry Association, Ye Jiaxing and Zheng Yuanxing, representing the Sausage Industry Association, and Zhang Pansun, representing the International Trade Bureau, attended the meeting. The concrete countermeasures are as follows: (1) First, assess the amount of Philippine goods imported into China. If the amount of Chinese goods exported to the Philippines is greater, then the strategy will be to increase the import tax on Philippine goods as a countermeasure. (2) The relevant commercial associations will state their countermeasures and send them to the City Chamber of Commerce for reference, and then the City Chamber of Commerce will forward them. (3) Notify the United States, pay attention to Sino-American relations, and persuade the Philippine government not to implement the tax increase. (4) Suggest that the government revise the tariff on Philippine goods in order to counter them.

Japan's Foreign Trade Surplus in August 138

Due to Sharp Drop in Japanese Exchange Rate

The Japanese Commercial Counselor's Office in Shanghai received a telegram from its home country yesterday stating that Japan's export trade in August was worth 136 million yen. Since the sharp drop in the Japanese exchange rate, exports of raw silk, cotton cloth, and silk have increased greatly. On the contrary, imports of goods, except for cotton and machinery, have decreased. Therefore, the result of foreign trade in this month was a surplus of 63 million yen. However, since the beginning of this year, the total deficit in foreign trade has still reached more than 160 million yen.

Bomb in Scrap Copper 139

Steelworker Blows Off Half of His Right Hand

Wu Xiquan, a 50-year-old man from Pudong, runs a coppersmith shop at No. 81 Zhangjia Lane, outside Xiaonanmen in Nanshi. The day before yesterday, Wu bought several catties of scrap copper from his colleague Zhu Hongsheng, who lives in Zhabei, and brought it back to his shop. However, there was a bomb in the scrap copper. Wu did not notice. Yesterday morning at about 9:00 a.m., Wu was crushing the scrap copper with an iron hammer in order to melt it and turn it into copper utensils. Unexpectedly, there was a loud bang that shook the sky and the earth. Residents nearby heard the sound and were surprised and rushed to the shop to check. They saw Wu in a daze on the ground, and the upper half of his right hand had been blown off by the bomb. The scene was tragic. People took Wu to the hospital for treatment. According to the doctor, the injury was not fatal, but after the injury heals, the right hand will be disabled.

Huang Boqiao Discusses Renewal Plan for City Ferry 141

City Public Enterprise Economic Committee to Meet Next Week

Recently, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau has spared no effort in rectifying the Pudong ferry business. Yesterday, a Central News Agency reporter asked Huang Boqiao, the director of the Public Utilities Bureau, about this matter. According to him, the city ferry currently has four cross-river ferries: 1. From Dongmen Road to Dongchang Road, 2. From Huishan Wharf to Qichangzhan, 3. From Dinghai Bridge to Qingning Temple, 4. From Wusong to Gaoqiao. The ferry equipment is also more thorough than the past commercial operations. However, improvements are still being sought. It is planned to build new-style double-ended ferries and to use oil for combustion. In addition, there are also four ferries between Tongren Wharf and Gaoqiao, which run once every hour. However, there are more passengers on Sundays or other holidays, so it is crowded. If the machinery is damaged, there is a concern that the service will be suspended. Therefore, it is planned to build another ferry in the near future for use on Sundays, holidays, or when the machinery is damaged. Long-distance ferries are also being planned. The municipal government originally had an organization called the City Business Economic Committee last year, and the rules of the committee have also been announced. The first meeting can be convened approximately next week. At that time, all of the bureau's plans for public business will be submitted for discussion. I was given the rules of the committee, so I have copied them as follows:

Rules of the Shanghai Municipal Government Public Enterprise Economic Committee Article 1: This committee is organized by the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, the directors of the bureaus in charge of public enterprises, the director of the Finance Bureau, and the general manager of the City Bank. The Secretary-General is the chairman, all appointed by the Mayor. Article 2: The members of this committee are honorary positions. Article 3: The term of office of the members of this committee is the same as their term of office in their original positions. Article 4: The tasks of this committee are as follows: (1) To propose the establishment of new public enterprises; (2) To review the principles for establishing new public enterprises; (3) To review the plans for expanding existing public enterprises; (4) To plan the expenses required for public enterprises; (5) To review the economic reports of public enterprises; (6) To study other economic issues related to public enterprises. Article 5: This committee shall hold a regular meeting once every two months after the end of each half-year to receive reports from various public enterprises on the past half-year. Temporary meetings shall be convened when necessary by the Mayor, the Chairman, or at the request of the members in charge of the public enterprises. Article 6: This committee may temporarily hire relevant experts to participate in discussions for reference in solving specialized problems, and pay appropriate fees after the matter is completed. Article 7: When this committee holds a meeting, the personnel directly responsible for operating the public enterprises may attend the meeting to report or express their opinions, but they have no voting rights. Article 8: This committee must have all members present to discuss and decide on the tasks of Article 4, paragraphs 1 to 4. A unanimous decision by all members is required. If a member is unable to attend due to special circumstances, they should entrust another member in writing to represent them with full authority. Article 9: The Chairman shall carry out the review of reports, the resolution of methods, the reporting to the Mayor for approval, or the execution by the competent bureau. Article 10: The secretarial and recording affairs of this committee shall be handled by personnel dispatched by the Secretariat of the Municipal Government. Article 11: Matters not covered in these rules may be amended at any time. Article 12: These rules shall come into effect on the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

Highway near Hui and Ning Road: Robbery, Police and Thieves Exchange Fire 142

No One Injured, Three Thieves Escape

Li Sixuan, a local, has operated the Ding He Tai tobacco and paper store at number 417 Hui Ning Road in the second district of Nanshi for many years. Business was said to be decent. He robbed fifty-six yuan in cash and over three hundred jiao in fractional currency from the counter and attempted to flee with the loot. He fired two shots as a warning while exiting. Unexpectedly, the back door of the store connected to Huai Ren Li. A police officer on patrol named Wang Fenglou was stationed inside the lane. Finally, as the police officer pursued relentlessly, the three thieves turned around and fired two more shots. Officer Wang then fired five shots in quick succession. Both sides were extremely flustered, so no one was injured. At that time, Officer Wang knew he only had one bullet left in his gun, so he could not continue the pursuit. The three thieves narrowly escaped. Afterwards, the victim, accompanied by Officer Wang, filed a report to the Second District Headquarters requesting an investigation.

Zhabei Pawnshop to Refund Robbery Losses 144

Social Affairs Bureau Approves Proportional Distribution Based on Pawn Ticket Value

Pawning Customers Allowed to Inspect the Inventory at Any Time

Since the January 28th Incident, the people's economy has suffered greatly. The pawnshop industry, especially those located in Zhabei, has been robbed extensively, seriously impacting the finances of the poor. Previously, the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau received reports of robberies from pawnshops such as Dingsheng on Gonghe Xin Road, Zengshun on Guoqing Road, and Dekang on North Sichuan Road in Zhabei. However, because the Japanese troops had not yet withdrawn at that time, officials were unable to investigate, and the truth remained unclear. To be cautious, the Bureau ordered each pawnshop to submit a signed statement. The statement said, "If the reported robbery situation of the pawnshop is false, we are willing to accept punishment." The Bureau approved the filing and, in accordance with Article 22 of the Shanghai Pawnshop Business Regulations, ordered that pawned items with receipts be redeemed as usual. Remaining unreceipted pawned items should be sold, with half the proceeds going to the pawnshop and half distributed proportionally to the pawning customers based on the value of the pawn tickets. It is said that for Dingsheng Pawnshop, each one yuan of the pawn ticket will get 2 fen for the pawning customer. The Zengshun Pawnshop paid out 4 fen per yuan for the pawning customers. The Dekang Pawnshop paid 3 fen per yuan for the pawning customers. Furthermore, stamped copies of the robbery inventory were issued for pawning customers to inspect and verify at any time.

This petitioner married the defendant as a second wife on October 13th of the 19th year of the Republic of China through matchmaker Shen Lianxiang. The wedding was held in Ningbo, and we returned to our residence in Shanghai three days later. Sometimes, if there were any disputes, the defendant would become enraged and gather many people to beat and injure this petitioner. Later, after persuasion from relatives and friends, the matter was settled. The defendant admitted her mistakes and repented, so this petitioner also hoped to settle the matter and make peace, hoping that the couple would return to harmony. Unexpectedly, the defendant suddenly ran away on her own on April 11th of last year, taking with her soft luggage, clothes, jewelry, and other items, estimated to be worth over 1,500 yuan. This petitioner reported this to the police station at the time, and there is a record. This petitioner repeatedly inquired and finally learned that the defendant had fled back to Ningbo. He repeatedly sent people to urge her to return home, but she ignored them. This petitioner then hired a lawyer to send a letter of inquiry and persuasion, but the defendant still ignored it. It was not until July 23rd of this year that Tu Shaowen and others were persuaded to persuade Zhao Anlan to propose a divorce to this petitioner, willing to return the gold jewelry and other items taken away that year. This petitioner thought that ordinary middle-class families spend their hard-earned savings over the years to marry a wife and start a family, which is not easy. When marrying the defendant, all the expenses for the wedding and goods cost about 4,000 yuan. Once divorced, it would be like the family being destroyed. If he remarries, he does not know when to wait, would it not be both a loss of people and money? After thinking it over again and again, how could he be willing? Therefore, this petitioner petitions the court to summon the defendant to the court and order her to compensate for the expenses before and after the wedding and the clothes and other items taken away, totaling 4,080 yuan, to protect his rights and maintain humanity. It would be virtuous and convenient." The court granted the petition and a hearing will be held soon.

Investigation into Stolen Components of Fire Hydrants 151

The Shanghai South District Firefighting Association oversees the installation of hundreds of fire hydrants in the streets and alleys and roads within the four districts of the southeast, northwest, and north. These hydrants are specifically designed to facilitate firefighting in the event of a fire. In recent years, the iron covers of the water tanks on all fire hydrants have been frequently stolen by thieves, and this has become increasingly outrageous. The copper screws on the fire hydrant openings have also been chiseled off and stolen, affecting more than 30 locations. The copper screws are the most critical components for connecting the leather hoses during firefighting. Once stolen, the hydrant becomes unusable, causing significant harm to the local area. The Firefighting Association has petitioned the Public Security Bureau to order its subordinate district offices to investigate and punish the perpetrators. In addition, local residents near the installed fire hydrants are advised to pay extra attention. Anyone who witnesses the theft of copper screws or water tank iron covers from the fire hydrant openings, regardless of who they are, is permitted to hand them over to the police on duty for investigation, so as to eliminate local hazards and protect the public safety of the people.

Recent News on the Photographic Printing of the Song Dynasty Qishazang Buddhist Canon 155

The translation and circulation of Buddhist scriptures in China initially relied on handwritten copies, then stone carvings, and then wood carvings. Printing became more convenient and circulation became more widespread. This was particularly prevalent during the Song dynasty, such as the Shu edition of the Northern Song dynasty, the Dongchan Temple edition of Fuzhou, the Kaiyuan Temple edition of Fuzhou in the Southern Song dynasty, the Wang Yongcong edition of Sixi, the Zifu Temple edition of Sixi, and the Yansheng Monastery edition of Qisha, all of which were famous among the versions. However, today, if one wants to see its remnants, the Shu edition is as rare as a phoenix, and even the other five editions from Dongchan onwards are either found in domestic and foreign collections or have been recorded in books as a small number of fragments without a large part, or later generations have supplemented the editions instead of the original edition. Now, the Qishazang Buddhist Canon, which is photographed and printed in Shanghai, is a complete set and the original edition. The photographs capture the original stones, and the authenticity is preserved, which greatly satisfies the wishes of researchers and practitioners around the world. The origin of the Qishazang Collection: During the Duanping period of the Song dynasty (1234 AD), the Buddhist nun Hongyuan of the Yansheng Monastery in Qisha, Pingjiang, cut off her arm and raised funds to publish the entire collection of sutras, precepts, and treatises. It was not completed until the Zhida period of Emperor Wuzong of the Yuan dynasty. This is a rough overview. The original version is in the form of palm leaves. The collection of the Wolong and Kaiyuan Temples in Xi'an is now preserved by the Shaanxi Provincial Library. Last year, Mr. Zhu Qinglan discovered it during disaster relief and assigned Fan Cheng to investigate it in detail. Each page has five sides, each side has six lines, and each line has seventeen characters. It has the nianhao of Jiaxi (1237 AD) and Chunyou (1241 AD). Ye Gongchuo, Jiang Weiqiao, Di Baoxian, Xu Naichang, Ding Fubao, Huang Yichang, Wu Zhaozeng, Li Jingwei, Li Yuanjing, and others all believed that this was the most perfect complete collection of ancient Chinese editions, which fortunately survived for 600 years. It must contribute greatly to the world's culture and art. It was then decided to photograph, print, and distribute it, and the Shanghai Photographic Printing Song Edition Tibetan Sutra Society was organized in Shanghai (the office is located on the fourth floor of Bao'an Fang, Damalu, Shanghai Public Concession) to be responsible for handling it. The Buddhist Bookstore (located in Ren'an Lane, Guling Road, Shanghai Public Concession) is responsible for all distribution matters. The work of compiling and proofreading the scriptures, collecting missing leaves, and ordering printing paper has made considerable progress. Previously, photography technicians and editorial staff were selected and sent to Shaanxi, where Li Shouting and Fan Cheng supervised the photography of glass slides, which is actively underway. It is expected to print 500 copies, each with more than 6,300 volumes, which will be published in stages and completed in three years. The advance purchase price is 525 yuan, paid in full at one time. A notice will be published in the newspaper soon. The reporter has seen the original scriptures, with elegant characters, exquisite engraving, few errors, and the ability to correct errors in later editions. The images of Buddhas listed at the beginning of the volumes are especially solemn and beautiful. The writers and engravers of the day wrote their wishes and signed their names, containing merit, which is different from the simplicity of other books. Studying and reciting it will sweep away secular obstacles. Libraries, academic organizations, and temples are expected to rush to order it.

Mr. Tao Qisheng, a famous doctor from Fengjing, specializes in treating internal and external complicated diseases, and is particularly skilled in treating throat wind carbuncles and other ailments. This spring, Mr. Tao came to Shanghai to avoid hardship. He casually treated illnesses among friends and relatives, and all recovered quickly. As a result, his reputation as a good doctor quickly spread throughout Shanghai. This came to the attention of Yan He, Zhou Shoujuan, Ding Song, Pan Yihua and other figures in literary and art circles, who then persuaded Mr. Tao to open a clinic in Shanghai. Mr. Tao, with a benevolent heart and desire to help people, deeply agreed with Mr. Yan and others' proposal. Therefore, he established a clinic at the Nanshi Doujia Street Noodle Industry Association. In addition, because of the requests from various circles in Fengjing, he decided to practice in both places, with a temporary stay of five days in each location.

Free Talk

Words of Old Man Ma Xiangbo, Ninety-Three Years Old

Glimpses of the Ten Commandments 172

— Jing Ji

Old Man Xiang advocated using the Ten Commandments, not starting from the time of national crisis: On the National Humiliation Memorial Day, May 7, 1916, he also lectured in the Central Park of Beijing. Now, a few excerpts are selected to show a glimpse of the content.

Now let's talk about the Sixth Commandment, "Thou shalt not commit adultery": that is, the most difficult marriage problem to solve now. "Marriage as husband and wife is a lifelong agreement to grow old together. If they abandon each other halfway, they are directly committing a great sin of disloyalty, dishonesty, unkindness, and injustice to humanity. Therefore, if adultery is committed, it is only right to separate and sleep in different rooms."

"Our country also knows that men and women living together is the greatest human relationship. How can the greatest relationship be changed every morning and evening? It is also known that if there is no distinction between husband and wife, it is close to being beasts; however, women who are suitable for sons borrow from friends and it is passed on as a good story! Everyone says: All evils start with lust; as for watching lewd plays and reading lewd books, they think of it as a pastime. Who knows that new scholars are opening up a new situation, saying that human beings are originally beasts, why bother to adhere to etiquette: isn't this the brand new situation in our country?"

"Gentlemen, in your opinion, should it be maintained or not?"

"As recorded in history books and reported in newspapers, both in ancient times and now, it is always the same. It can be seen that a woman would rather be killed than be raped; then, to rape one more woman is tantamount to killing one more person. Some people euphemistically call it 'taking a concubine'. Where is the affection? It is only for your stinky skin and stinky lust! If you say that you are doting on your concubine, you are actually taking away her freedom, destroying her personality, losing her shame, and extinguishing her spiritual light. You say I bought it with money, is it possible that people are for sale?"

"The Gospel of Matthew says: Whoever entices young children, it would be better to take a millstone and hang it around his neck and sink him to the bottom of the sea! It is as if to say that the evil of that person should not be allowed to live on the earth!"

Sketches of Nanjing 173

— Shi Ying

Various Aspects丨

In the dazzling organs and public offices, high-ranking officials with broad minds and fat bodies come in and out, as do arrogant section chiefs and haggard and dejected junior staff. The high-ranking officials seem not to care about coming and going; the middle-ranking ones are spirited and lively; and the junior staff are worried and hurried.

XXX

In the sky, airplanes, the means of transportation of the twentieth century, come and go; on Zhongshan Road, bright and fast cars speed by. On the muddy stone roads, dilapidated horse-drawn carts bump along; perhaps the wheelbarrow, which was invented before the era, squeaks and moves like a mournful cry.

XXX

The newly built official residences are all palace-style, resplendent and magnificent. But the entire layout and furnishings inside are completely Western, beautiful and comfortable. This is called "two difficulties are combined, and four beauties are combined." I remember Premier Sun Yat-sen saying that "the national revolution is the integration of China and the West"; the Three Principles of the People also draw extensively from ancient Chinese thought and follow modern Western modernism. Even architecture, a minor detail, is the same.

XXX

The thatched huts contrast each other; the long and clean Zhongshan Road contrasts with the roads that are "incense burners on sunny days and soy sauce vats on rainy days". But alas, the asphalt on both sides of Zhongshan Road is long gone, the mud and sand have been exposed, and it is also aging.

XXX

The plank beds in the halal restaurants, the beautiful sights on the Qinhuai River, and the thugs of XX University can be called the "Three Wonders of the New Capital."

General Cai's Song 174

— Wu Dongyuan

Cai Tingkai. Heroic spirit. This little heart vows not to change. Squeeze out loyalty. Show the honest liver. Risking danger and entrusting life is extremely generous. Eight hundred brave soldiers share the enemy's hatred. The Great Wall will never be destroyed. An accident happened overnight. In a hurry, the army was formed and the powerful invaders were shocked. Millions of people rely on you. Winning by surprise cannot be defeated. Scolding the wind and clouds. Overturning the rivers and seas. Like a rapid flow of water.澎澎湃湃. Like a stone breaking into pieces. 砰砰磕磕. The earth collapses and the gods are frightened. Continue to work hard and build up prestige. One vertical and one horizontal sweep away the filth. Helping Shun has mountain spirits. Many water monsters flee. Forty-three battles have not diminished. Raising arms and shouting courage a hundredfold. Cut off half of the Wusong River. Bixue fills the iron armor. Traitors Wang Lun and Qin Gui. Rare goods can be sold.援兵 do not arrive, what to do? The lonely army is in danger. How many times have we been facing each other with firm walls? Yafu's camp is still there. One army is a national teacher. Defeat the few with the many and occupy the important points. 丸泥 plug the barrier. Make the whole river into a road. Who can harm you if you walk on dangerous ground as if it were flat ground? Alas, the heroic spirit. Cai Tingkai, the commander of the Nineteenth Route Army.

Analysis of Shanghai People 175

— Bai Shi

Old Brands Few丨Fake Brands Many丨

The so-called Shanghai people are not actually Shanghai people. Real Shanghai people are called locals. Although there are no accurate statistics on the number of locals in Shanghai, according to ordinary estimates, they probably account for no more than 10%. The remaining 90%, although they include Cantonese, Ningbo people, Shandong people, Jiangbei people, and people from other remote border provinces, they all claim to be Shanghai people. So if you meet a guest who cannot speak a sentence of Shanghai dialect, just compliment him as a "Shanghai person", and you will never be wrong. Because of the mixture of people from all directions, "Shanghai dialect" is also greatly affected by "Shanghai people". The Shanghai dialect spoken by "locals" is actually authentic "Shanghai dialect", but "Shanghai people" insist that what the locals speak is Pudong dialect. The "Shanghai dialect" is a patchwork of dialects from various places. For example, "I" must be said like Ningbo people say "Ala"; "You" must be said like the locals say "侬"; "He" must be said like Suzhou people say "俚"; "Good" must be said like Cantonese say "顶括括"; "Bad" must be said like Northerners say "不兴": To express surprise and disappointment, one must say like Jiangbei people, "乖乖不得了". If your words can learn a sentence from the east and a sentence from the west like this, then people will be sincerely convinced and admire you as a genuine "Old Shanghai".

In the minds of "Shanghai people", it seems that Shanghai people are another ethnic group. Anyone who cannot speak this mixed-up "Shanghai dialect" is collectively called "乡下人", and the synonym for 乡下人 is called "阿木林" for the upper class and "屈死" for the lower class. In fact, today's "Shanghai" cannot even find a piece of brick, and today's concessions are the "countryside" of the former Shanghai. The current self-proclaimed old Shanghai people are actually authentic villagers. The villagers spoken of by Shanghai people may be new people from the city center.

Random Thoughts 176

— Luo Shui

Way Out Money Fight for Profit丨

(I)

In such a depressed society, it is simply impossible to talk about anything! Discussing the various problems of young people, such as seeking education, marriage, finding a career, and others, it takes a lot of effort to get a relatively satisfactory solution, but there is still no certainty, and failures are more common than successes! The depression of society can indeed affect one's outlook on life; those without knowledge certainly feel pain, but those with knowledge feel even more pain. Therefore, at present, there is only this way, that is, to try hard every day, no matter how difficult the problem is, and no matter how depressed the society is. In this way, maybe we can find a way out!

(II)

Seeking education requires money, marriage also requires money, and finding a career certainly requires money! Everything, everything, requires money, and it is impossible without money. In a society under this economic system, the power of money is higher than everything else, which is of course 丨The difference between "poverty-stricken walls" and "golden house hiding beauty" is only the amount of money! This can symbolically represent the present society as a whole. Therefore, those with money will have all their wishes fulfilled, and those without money will be told not to speak! Therefore, I advise you, for the way of money, you should explore it. It is much cheaper to have money after all.

(III)

Although society is depressed, the gentlemen and ladies who study "economics" are competing to be the first and the last, from the head of state to the common people, all are enthusiastically engaged in it. This kind of spirit is originally a good phenomenon, but the old master Mencius once said, "If superiors and inferiors compete for profit, the country is in danger!" As usual, it should be said that people who are enthusiastic about "economics" today should "retreat three times", but the fact is not so. Seeing profit bravely, the superiors follow the example of the inferiors, and they are still competing to be the first: as for the safety of the country, it seems to be another problem! Well, what is this phenomenon of national subjugation and species extinction?

Silver Silk, the Storytelling Rotary Club (9) 177

— Jiang Hongjiao

(V)

Mr. Wang, please take care of my house, I'll go out and buy some things and come back. Fenruo said.

"What are you buying? Today is the memorial monument unveiling ceremony, and all the shops on the street are closed for half a day." Mr. Wang said.

"He loves to eat melon. Eating melon makes him feel cooler, maybe it will make his illness better, that's his habit; and I also want to find Dr. Tang to give him an injection, I haven't been feeling very well these days either, if he's crazy for a few days, I can't stand it."

"I'm afraid Dr. Zhang is not at home? Everyone in town has gone to participate in this unveiling ceremony. But if you want melon, you definitely won't be able to buy it. I have two very big snow-fleshed watermelons left at home. Let me go back and bring them to him to eat."

"Okay, thank you! But, I should pay you for the melon."

"We've known each other for so many days, don't we even have the friendship of two watermelons? Sister-in-law! You're too serious." Mr. Wang said, putting on his long gown and leaving.

Less than ten minutes later, Fenruo was upstairs helping Yuan the madman finish his urination when someone knocked on the door downstairs.

"Mr. Wang! Why are you running so fast?" Fenruo welcomed Mr. Wang as she opened the door.

"Ah! Is it you?" Fenruo never expected a distinguished guest to arrive, and couldn't guess that he, whom she hadn't seen for more than ten years, had become a national hero worshiped by the whole country. Was she having an illusion, or was she dreaming? After she opened the door, she suddenly saw a military officer walking in very kindly.

"Fenruo, my Fenruo, it's still me, you certainly haven't completely forgotten your old friend. But, I've come too strangely today, it's certainly beyond your expectations." Regiment Commander Yuan closed the door and walked into the hall, and Fenruo followed him in.

"Then please sit down, Regiment Commander Yuan!" Fenruo poured him a cup of tea.

"You shouldn't have forgotten my name, Fenruo!"

"Yes, Mr. Yuan Renkai! I have already read your great name in the newspapers. How dare I call you by your name, such a hero as you are."

"You shouldn't have forgotten my old name, my Fenruo!"

"Please allow me to call you Mr. Yuan Renkai; otherwise I will call you Regiment Commander Yuan! Why bother to spend more brainpower thinking about things from more than ten years ago. Today in this town, a monument is being built for your achievements, waiting for you to perform the unveiling ceremony, why haven't you gone yet, everyone is waiting for you." Fenruo urged Regiment Commander Yuan to leave in a very solemn tone.

"Don't you let me sit for a while longer for such a rare opportunity?"

"Alas! Your future is bright, and it's not appropriate to sit in a widow's house for too long; I'm afraid that if news reporters find out and record it, it will be a whole page again. You should take care of yourself! Although I am also old, and my temples are gray."

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Words

Was Zheng Jicheng Guilty? 201

— Buddha

The death penalty for murderers is originally a most fair principle in criminal law. There is no disagreement about it in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. However, why was the murder committed? Why was one killed? There are reasons for it. They should be distinguished. We must examine the reasons and study the facts without rashly concluding that the murderer must die,

This time, Zhang Zongchang was assassinated by Zheng Jicheng at Jinan Station, so Zheng seemed to have deserved his crime. However, when Zhang Zongchang was in Shandong, his crimes against Shandong were obvious and well-known. The national government's arrest warrant has not been cancelled to this day. When the Shandong Provincial Government was in Tai'an, it also offered a reward of 50,000 yuan for his arrest. Zhang Zongchang originally deserved his crime to the Republic of China. Therefore, Zheng's killing of Zhang was actually eliminating harm for the country. He is not only innocent, but also deserves a reward. Therefore, Zheng should not have died. First.

Also, Zheng Jicheng confessed that if Zhang Zongchang had killed his uncle on the battlefield, that would be each for his master, and there would be nothing to say. However, Zhang ordered Jiang Mingyu to lure his uncle to Jinan, and after the brutal killing, he offered a reward of 30,000 yuan to go to Tianjin to capture him. He escaped twice by climbing over the wall. Zhang Zongchang not only killed his uncle Zheng Jinsheng, but also wanted to kill Zheng Jicheng to be rid of him quickly. Therefore, Zheng's assassination of Zhang was actually self-defense. If Zheng did not kill Zhang, Zhang would kill Zheng. What crime is there in self-defense? This is Zheng's second reason for not deserving to die.

National legislation exhausts reason to determine rewards and punishments, and uses facts to correct praise and criticism. It cannot use rigid articles and apply them to ever-changing facts. Therefore, what should be studied now is whether Zhang Zongchang is guilty. If Zhang Zongchang is indeed guilty, then Zheng's killing of Zhang should be considered legitimate, and cannot be considered an ordinary murder. If Zhang Zongchang is not guilty, then Zheng's killing of Zhang is naturally illegal. A murderer must die and cannot escape the law.

Science

The Art of Textile Printing 203

— Rui · Yu · Cheng ·

Printing is a form of partial dyeing, where desired patterns are made to appear on fabrics. It involves either creating patterns on undyed cloth or removing dye from specific areas of dyed cloth to reveal white patterns. But how is printing done? The key aspects are outlined below:

(A) Classified by Dye Properties:

(1) Mixing dye with an adhesive paste, so that the pattern adheres to the cloth. However, some dyes have a direct affinity for fibers, so they can be printed directly.

(2) Similarly, applying mordant dyes to fabrics that have been treated with a mordant.

(3) Applying dyes that develop color through post-treatment to the fabric, then passing it through a processing bath to develop the color.

(4) Dyeing the fabric first, either with a mordant or a preparatory treatment, then printing with chemicals to remove color from specific areas, or printing with non-coloring agents, followed by a treatment to develop color.

(5) Printing in a way that prevents certain areas from absorbing pigment, then passing it through a dye solution or mordant solution to develop the color.

(B) Classified by Mechanical Equipment:

(1) Printing with engraved rollers.

(2) Printing with engraved blocks.

Both of the above can be either raised or recessed.

(3) Block Pressing: Clamping the fabric between two engraved blocks, firmly securing it to prevent dye from penetrating.

(4) Tie-dyeing: Binding the fabric tightly at the patterned areas to prevent dye from penetrating.

(5) Cutting a paper stencil, then brushing dye paste onto the fabric; or using a stencil to prevent dye paste from being brushed on, before immersing it in dye solution. Or, on dyed fabrics, using a stencil to print with discharge paste and then processing it.

(6) Hand-painting to create the design.

Beyond these classifications, if classified by dyeing and printing processes, there are several other methods, generally distinguished by the color development method:

(1) Pigment Style: These pigments are not dyes that dissolve in water for immersion dyeing. Instead, they are painting pigments (Lake) mixed with a paste and printed onto the fabric surface. This method was mainly used for foreign label cloth in the past.

(2) Direct Printing Style: Using dyes that have a direct affinity for fibers, mixed into a suitable paste for printing. This method is applied to various fabrics.

(3) Steam Style: When applying mordant dyes for printing, the mordant and dye are mixed and printed, then steamed, allowing the two to combine and adhere to the fabric. This method can also be applied to various fabrics. When used with basic dyes, tannic acid must be added for fixation. If antimony salts are also used, it becomes even more durable. This method is exhaustively applied to plant fibers.

Antiques for Sale Opium Public Sale Paper Money Tax

Main: Similarly, printing with developing dyes, then passing them through a diazotization solution to develop color, also falls into this category.

(4) Madder or Dyed Style: Printing with a specific mordant, then immersing in a mordant dye to develop the color in that area.

(5) Resist Style: Printing with substances that resist coloration or prevent color development, then immersing or brushing with dye. After removing or washing off the resist, the areas appear white or undyed.

For example, applying a resist paste to fabric mordanted with beta-naphthol, to achieve a resist effect during color development, is called Resist Pad Style. It is used in printing mousseline.

(6) Discharge Style: This method is very important; dyed fabric is printed with color-removing or fading chemicals, revealing a white background or discharging other colors. This method is widely used on various fibers.

With recent advances in chemistry, in addition to the above, new dyeing methods are constantly being invented, creating unique patterns to satisfy people's desires. It is said that there are now methods that combine with the fabric's structure to produce exceptionally beautiful patterns. The civilization of material things is boundless!

Social Improvement Discussion Group

A Discussion on the Dining Problem 204

— Chou

Regarding the Improvement of the Dining Problem. Mr. Wen Jun of the Yi Yi Restaurant, and Messrs. Qi Xing and Zheng, have successively published many good suggestions in this journal. Now, based on the principles of economy and hygiene, I would like to offer my humble opinions for everyone to discuss:

1. Separated vs. Communal Dining

A. Advantages and Disadvantages of Communal Dining: It is convenient, efficient, allows for a greater variety of dishes, and can cater to different tastes. These are the advantages. However, it is unhygienic and easily spreads diseases. These are the disadvantages.

B. Advantages and Disadvantages of Separated Dining: The only advantage is that separated dining can avoid direct and indirect transmission of diseases. However, it is monotonous, troublesome, easily becomes cold in winter, and it is difficult to cater to different tastes with three or more people. These are the obvious disadvantages of separated dining. As far as the author knows, when Ms. Zhang Mojun was the head of a women's normal school in Nanjing, she implemented a separated dining system for a time, but soon reverted to communal dining. When Mr. Guo Hongsheng was the head of Nanjing Higher Normal School, he implemented a separated dining system for quite a long time, where each person received one dish and one soup, or one meat dish and one vegetable dish, served in specially made tin utensils with compartments. Although they had grown accustomed to it, many still complained. However, because the school provided the meals, and they were encouraged to prioritize hygiene, everyone tolerated it. But after Dongda (National Southeastern University) was established, students mostly managed their own meals, and this system gradually fell into disuse. From this, it can be seen that separated dining is difficult to implement. As for families implementing separated dining, nothing has been heard of it.

C. Feasible Solution: Since separated dining has difficulties in terms of habit and economy, as mentioned above, and communal dining has terrible drawbacks, I believe there is a feasible solution that can take the strengths of both Western (separated) and Eastern (communal) dining, without their drawbacks. That is, each person should have two pairs of chopsticks, two spoons, and a small plate or saucer, for separating food and soup when taking it. Everything else remains the same. This idea is similar to Mr. Qi Xing's suggestion. The dining hall of the General Hospital of the Red Cross Society in this city implements this system, and there is no difficulty in implementing it at all. Various societies, organizations, and families can emulate it.

2. Food Quality: For staple food, it is indeed better to have wheat and mixed grains. However, in this city, it may not be easy to advocate this immediately. I believe it would be good to change breakfast to a bowl of noodles for each person, which seems to be widely feasible. In recent years, students at Tongji, Zhonggong, and various universities who have meal packages all have a bowl of noodles for breakfast, and people from all over eat it, which can serve as evidence. As for dishes, it is better to have more vegetables than meat, and more fresh than pickled. I believe that the local health authorities or medical organizations should create and publish a dietary chart based on the principles of economy and hygiene for us to improve our diet. As for beverages, plain boiled water is best.

3. Cleaning of Bowls, Plates, Spoons, and Chopsticks: This issue is the core of reforming the dining problem. After each meal, a dedicated person should be responsible for or supervise the cleaning. They must be washed with boiling water! It is best to boil them all in a pot! Otherwise, the spread of disease will still be difficult to avoid, which is equivalent to not making any changes!

4. The Kitchen Cleaning Cloth: Germs from typhoid fever, cholera, dysentery, and other dangerous diseases can often be transmitted from the market vegetables to the kitchen, from the cook's hands to the cleaning cloth, and from the cleaning cloth to the bowls, plates, spoons, and chopsticks! Then they go straight into the mouth! Special attention must be paid! Washing them after use is not enough; they must be boiled!

School Photo

A Glimpse Inside the Dining Hall 205

— Thirteen-Year-Old

"The side dishes are terrible today. How are we supposed to eat with this?"

Amidst the clamor in the dining hall of XX School, student XXX said at the dining table. A then added, "As long as everyone contributes ten cents, six people have sixty cents, adding two bowls of dishes, isn't the problem solved?"

"Bah!," another fat person said, "I don't even have the money for ice cream today, and it's hot. You want to add more dishes?"

"Then what should we do? Not having good side dishes isn't good business," XX said sadly.

"Hmm!" a strategist said after a while, "Who will catch a fly? Wait until the side dishes are almost finished, then put the fly at the bottom of the bowl, and then go to the kitchen to question them. That will do it!"

So XX ran out with a smile, and soon brought one back (its origin is unknown; perhaps it came from the latrine) and gave it to the strategist.

Thus 丨 so 丨 the negotiation was settled.

Five minutes later, the cook brought in a steaming bowl of dishes. People at other tables saw it and salivated. XX then said,

"As expected, you live up to your reputation, you are indeed a Han Xin of the sheep country."

A Corner of Society

Wanting to Be a Godmother 206

— Zhou · ·

The neighbors across the way have been arguing these past few days. After inquiring, it turned out that a joke had turned serious. This is truly the work of mediocre people!

A sister-in-law who lives in the attic room recently came from the countryside. While chatting with the landlady of the second floor in the guest room, she mentioned that she had a godmother in the countryside. Upon hearing this, the landlady became interested. She was naturally fond of small talk, so she said with a smile to the sister-in-law in the attic room, "That's good. You have a godmother in the countryside, so have one in Shanghai too. How about recognizing me as your godmother?"

The sister-in-law in the attic room knew that she was just making small talk, so she smiled and pretended to agree. However, the landlady took it seriously and started calling her "dear baby" and "sweetheart" without any reservations. She even wanted her to formally recognize her as her godmother on a chosen day. This put the sister-in-law in the attic room in an awkward position, because it was impossible to do so in reality. Generally, a godmother should be older in age, but she was more than ten years younger than the goddaughter. This kind of reversed kinship was a big joke. However, the landlady would not let it go, so the matter became difficult. Fortunately, the sister-in-law in the attic room understood. "Asking someone is not a loss. It's just a roll of the tongue." Since she was so eager to be a godmother, she would recognize her. Sure enough, on a certain day, she performed the ceremony like dry sons and daughters worshiping their dry parents. The whole thing was as ridiculous as a stage play!

But a godmother must have the rights of a godmother. Fortunately, this landlady had plenty of money. After giving the sister-in-law a "meeting fee," she also lavishly prepared a banquet to invite her goddaughter. At this time, everyone was happy. But the disastrous thing happened afterward.

According to custom, the goddaughter also had to prepare a meal to reciprocate the godmother. However, the sister-in-law in the attic room did not have much money and could not afford a lavish banquet. She could only use the four yuan she had received to prepare a simple meal. But the godmother would not agree. She insisted on having a banquet costing more than ten yuan. As a result, things went sour and they turned against each other. They forgot about the godmother and goddaughter relationship and started scolding each other loudly. Both of them were Ningbo natives, so their voices were particularly loud, and their art of scolding was especially skillful, causing a commotion throughout the alley.

It is now rumored that the sister-in-law in the attic room will definitely move out tomorrow morning, because they have been arguing for three days in a row and can no longer live together.

Alas! Not wanting to live a peaceful life, they looked for trouble to create a commotion. What a pity! Ah! This kind of thing can only happen in the alleys of Shanghai.
